Revenue and Expenditure of Various Agencies Shall Be Handled Uniformly by the National Treasury 46

(Nanjing) The revenue and expenditure of various central agencies shall be handled uniformly by the National Treasury. The four measures are as follows: 1. The direct revenue of the central ministries and committees, the revenue of their affiliated non-business agencies, and the surplus of their affiliated business agencies or the apportioned non-business expenses shall be submitted to the National Treasury for verification and collection. 2. The expenses of the central ministries and committees and their affiliated agencies shall be planned and issued by the National Treasury. 3. The central ministries and committees and their affiliated business and non-business agencies shall prepare a ten-day report form of expenditure income and send it to the Ministry of Finance every ten days. 4. The Ministry of Finance shall, in conjunction with the relevant ministries and committees, formulate measures based on the first three principles and submit them to the Executive Yuan for approval and promulgation. (10th Special Dispatch)

The Beijing Municipal Social Affairs Bureau Pays Attention to Preventing Roundworm Infection 47

(Nanjing) The Health Education Committee of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has learned that students in various schools have been suffering from roundworm disease recently. After consultation, the Department of Health's Parasite Group was asked to test them. A collection of 10,000 student stool samples from primary and secondary schools was solicited, from October last year to the end of the year. A total of 3,872 stool samples were received. The results of the tests showed that 1,328 people were infected with roundworm disease. The Department of Health has specially made roundworm pills, sent them to the meeting for distribution and treatment, and is also studying the causes of roundworm occurrence, transmission routes, symptoms, treatment methods, prevention methods, etc., and printing and distributing leaflets to make everyone pay attention. (10th Special Dispatch)

Page 7

Current Commentary

Resistance and Struggle by Hui 58

1. The Meaning of Resistance

Since the September 18th Incident, the entire nation has been talking about resistance and everyone has been saying that only resistance can lead to survival. It seems that our resistance alone is enough to make the enemy fear and no longer advance. If we resist again, the lost territory of the Northeast can be recovered, and the past national humiliations can be eliminated. Therefore, there is even more talk of "long-term resistance," believing that this can encourage the people of the country and also slightly ease the enemy's threat. However, one year and four months have passed since the incident. The occupation of Shenyang and the fall of Jinzhou have not been recovered. Among them, only the Battle of Shanghai was where we suffered unprecedented losses, but we were not humiliated and still had the qualifications for equal peace talks. The resistance in Jilin and Heilongjiang has only left behind bloody historical traces, waiting for future liquidation.

Resistance means that when the enemy comes to attack, we resist. Then the situation of the host and guest is different. People are active, and we are passive, with no room for self-determination. If people don't come to attack, we will waste troops and food and be unable to do anything. It's like being trapped in a besieged city, with hungry people inside and strong bandits outside, seeking temporary peace but without long-term plans. No mistake in planning is greater than this. Moreover, resistance is purely a passive attitude, conservative rather than progressive. In today's world, not only are all things progressing and changing rapidly, but all countries are also seeking accelerated development. To plan a country while being conservative is impossible even in times of peace, let alone when a strong enemy has already entered the country.

2. Speaking of Resistance Now is Like Locking the Stable After the Horse is Gone

The enemy wants to gradually erode our country, occupying a place today and cutting off a city tomorrow, using the excuse of security and talking about peace. They also declare to the world that "China is not a modern country and has no modern organization," so it can be cut off at will. If we only talk about resistance, we lack a whole and planned organization and only use the force of a local part to resist the enemy's entire army. The number of wins and losses is not something that needs to be divined.

Moreover, the three northeastern provinces are the richest in East Asia. In a single day, we actually lost them. Even if we try to preserve everything and crave peace, the enemy will send out iron cavalry to attack cities and seize land. Jinzhou has already been lost, and the land of the key pass of Jiujiang is also in danger. If we continue to be trapped here, how can we save ourselves? The enemy deceives us that our strength is weak and will definitely compromise to seek reconciliation. They do not know that the more we seek temporary preservation and hope for peace, the more the enemy will advance and attack fiercely. Even if we let them run rampant, we may not be able to achieve peace.

For example, the statement issued by the Japanese army authorities on December 23 last year regarding our country's Third Plenary Session not only disregarded international friendship but also went to the extreme of insults. The concluding words said, "The first means to maintain peace in the Far East at the present is to liquidate the extremely dangerous Chinese Kuomintang and its foreign policy." These words are even worse than the phrase "drink horses in Wu Mountain". Can we endure to the end and only talk about resistance?

3. The Meaning of Struggle

Our country has been weak for a long time. However, it has a vast territory and a large population, and it is richly endowed by nature. If there is active leadership, turning defeat into victory is not difficult. The enemy's national strength is exhausted. Judging from the national budget of 2.23 billion yen for this year alone, they cannot afford it. The accumulation of its national debt has reached 10 billion yen. If they increase their troops to China again, each increase of a division will add at least 30 million yen in military expenses. For a formal war against China, if they send 100 divisions, the annual cost will be at least 5 billion yen. With the enemy's current national strength, they will deplete one-twentieth of their national wealth in one year. Even if they win the war, they will undoubtedly be the second Germany after the European war.

Taking the lessons of the January 28 Shanghai War as an example, we were able to fight the enemy for as long as thirty-two days with inferior forces and defeated weapons. If we have a whole plan and full mobilization, even if the national defense is completely lacking and the fortresses are completely lost, we can make great sacrifices and fight the enemy for five or ten years. Then we will have the surplus strength, and the enemy will die on its own. From afar, like Napoleon's invasion of Russia, and more recently, like the six Japanese divisions' invasion of Siberia, the Russians did not talk about resistance, but only strove to fight, causing the enemy to retreat due to internal frustration, and thus consolidating their national foundation. Moreover, in today's situation, so-called justice must have strength in order to be able to implement what it says. If the forces between countries are not equal, then there is no justice to speak of. Justice is something that changes with strength. If you want to strengthen your country's power, you must actively struggle.

4. The Future of Struggle and the Realization of Reality

The reason why Japan dares to inch forward and continue to invade us is that it deceives our people and has no spirit of struggle. If we can truly mobilize the entire country and rise up in a battle, and strive for the national revolutionary spirit and struggle for a hundred years of history, then how can the enemy, which is like the setting sun in the west, engage in a protracted war? The past events of Alsace-Lorraine being cut off can be learned. The hatred of Poland's subjugation and territorial division has been avenged. We have a land area of 3,444,300 square miles and a population of over 400 million. If we struggle desperately, how can the enemy own the Northeast region?

Moreover, the undisguised aggression of Japanese imperialism has aroused the conflict of interests among capitalist countries. Once they wage war against us, the 300 million yen of exports to China will be completely cut off, and the import of over 200 million yuan of industrial raw materials will be severely affected. In addition, with the expenditure of huge military expenses, how can its extremely poor people bear it?

Therefore, China today, if it wants to establish a nation and survive, should not deal with things superficially again, engage in passive and inactive resistance, and grow the enemy's arrogance. The urgent task at present is to have an accurate understanding of reality. Do not be overly afraid of the enemy's military power. Rise up and make a national struggle to the death. Only struggle can achieve survival. Only struggle can protect our nation. The great disaster is now before us, and the catastrophe is close at hand. We can endure no more and concede no more. An urgent struggle is the only way out.

Soviet Russia Pays Attention to Armed Defense Against Strong Neighbors Invading 59

Large Factories Converted into Arms Factories

Industrial Plans Slightly Delayed

(Moscow) When the plenary session of the Central Executive Committee of the Communist Party opened on Saturday, Stalin gave a fiery speech. The contents were not released until tonight, generally saying that the war crisis in the Far East forced the Soviet Russia to convert several large factories into military factories to prepare for contingencies. Therefore, the production in the last year of the Five-Year Plan will inevitably be delayed. However, the Soviet Russia now has the latest weapons to cope with unexpected events. Although Stalin did not explicitly mention Japan, he said that the Soviet Russia had to change several factories because a certain neighboring country refused to sign a non-aggression treaty. The neighboring country he mentioned was obviously Japan. Stalin also said that our factories will soon become factories that produce national defense equipment. The country is now ready to cope with all war dangers. The initial war crisis forced us to develop heavy industry at an extremely rapid pace. Today, we have the preparation to resist attacks, and this heavy industry can be slightly slowed down in the second five years. In the past, the Soviet Russia could be said to have no self-defense. Today, it can actually provide the Red Army with the most sophisticated defense equipment without limitation. (9th National Electricity)

Our Protest to Japan Has Been Sent to the League of Nations

The Japanese Army's Invasion of Yuguan is a Planned Project 60

(Geneva) The Chinese government informed the League of Nations that the recent unprovoked attack and occupation of Shanhaiguan by Japan was entirely a premeditated plan. Japanese Imperialism's War Preparations Mania 64

Land, Sea, and Air Forces Preparing for Large-Scale Maneuvers to Threaten the US and Russia

Nationwide Mobilization Plan Even Extends to Dogs and Horses

Special Dispatch from China United Press, Tokyo - Japanese imperialism's current war preparations have reached a state of intense mania. Last year, the land, sea, and air forces held several unprecedented large-scale exercises. Extending into this year, the Japanese land and naval authorities, recognizing the urgency of the war crisis, are preparing to conduct various more important special maneuvers. The special maneuvers, which are held annually, have decided that the Kanazawa and other nine divisions, the Zentsuji Eleventh Division, and a mixed brigade will participate, and will be held in the Fukui Prefecture area. The Hokuriku region, including Ishikawa, Fukui, and Toyama, faces the Soviet Union across the Sea of Japan. Therefore, these maneuvers are of particularly important significance for attacking the Soviet Union. Before these maneuvers, it has been decided to hold special air force maneuvers. This air force unit is filled with content by exploiting money from the broad masses of laborers under the false pretense of patriotic donations. Japanese imperialism uses this money to expand and improve its new-style killing aviation weapons, preparing to further sacrifice the blood of the toiling masses and attack and slaughter the toiling masses of other countries. The participating units in the special air force maneuvers have decided to use six aircraft squadrons, six flight schools, one anti-aircraft artillery unit, and 400 aircraft, in the central and northern regions of Shizuoka and Aichi, in addition to the Sixth Regiment in Pyongyang, Korea. At the same time, on the naval side, various new-style warships, aircraft, etc. have been completed, and it has been decided to conduct unprecedented large-scale naval exercises in the South Sea Islands and Ogasawara Islands area for approximately one month in June this year. The main active weapons are naval aircraft, new-style cruisers, submarines, etc. The purpose is to spy on the Soviet Union, further divide China, and at the same time target American imperialism, which goes without saying. After American imperialism concentrated its fleet in the Pacific and held naval maneuvers, it did not disperse the fleet, but kept it concentrated in one place. Japanese imperialism's naval maneuvers are clearly intended to demonstrate force to American imperialism.

On the army side, in order to attack the Soviet Union and further divide China, from December 19th to 22nd last year, it convened a secret meeting of 260 battalion commanders, group secretaries, etc., from infantry, cavalry, artillery, flight corps, regiment commanders, engineer corps, transport corps, heavy artillery independent battalions across the country, and decided on a major reform of the troops. In order to implement national mobilization, the military mobilized retired soldiers, youth training center students, youth league members, and female youth league members nationwide, and investigated: ㈠ the operational processes of the 30-year plan for military administration, ㈡ changes in horse production resources, ㈢ the progress of horse improvement, ㈣ facilities related to horses and their effects. On November 29th, they implemented horse purchases nationwide in unison, compiling them for military use. Dogs were also trained for military use. Lieutenant General Oshima Yoshimasa is the president of the "Imperial Military Dog Association," and training centers have been established in Toyama and Yoyogi to carry out the breeding, training, and propagation of various military working dogs, as well as to implement the registration of improved dog breeds and pedigree certification. The nationwide mobilization plan extends to dogs and horses. The scale and thoroughness of the plan are such as this.

The Japanese imperialists' efforts to prepare for a major war have reached a fever pitch. An unprecedented war to attack the Soviet Union, divide China, and massacre the laboring masses is becoming increasingly imminent, advocating youthful war thought.

The Chaotic Situation in Jilin 81

(Japanese Suppressive Policies)

(Combining Force and Deviousness)

Since the Japanese traitor Mutō took office in Jilin, he has changed his policy of solely relying on forceful suppression. He now also employs insidious methods of division. The following is a summary of the key aspects:

㈠ Recruiting and Surrendering Righteous Armies: Since mid-December of last year, the Japanese traitors in various counties and towns have widely posted notices to recruit and accept the surrender of our righteous armies. The Jilin Municipal Garrison Commander, Ji Xing, and Xi Qia put their names to these notices, stating that anyone surrendering a large rifle would receive 30 national currency units, a small rifle 20 units, and surrendering empty-handed would earn 10 units. After surrendering their weapons, each person would be given a "Good Citizen Certificate" and those desiring service would be considered for enrollment.

㈡ Policies of Recruiting and Surrendering: The policies of recruiting and surrendering generally employed a method of starting from nearby areas and extending to more distant ones. Counties in the hinterland of Jilin, such as Yitong, Yushu, Shulan, Shuangcheng, Acheng, Panshi, Dehui, Changchun, Yongji, etc., and various locations along the railway lines initially had righteous armies everywhere in mid-August of last year. Now, there is not a single trace of them left.

㈢ The Vicious Tactic of "Catching the King to Catch the Thieves": The Japanese traitors, after incorporating our righteous armies, would offer small favors to the soldiers to trick them into surrendering their weapons. The leaders would then be falsely accused of crimes, put to death, or secretly assassinated to eliminate future troubles. Those who have died include Lin Zhonghao, Sanjianghao, Xiaoshuangsheng, Chang Zuo, Wu Deng, etc.

㈣ The Recent Conditions of Our Righteous Armies: Except for the major righteous armies led by Wang Delin and Ding Li, which have received some limited assistance, most of the other smaller units in Jilin have been fighting for years. They are severely lacking in weapons, ammunition, and clothing. In this severe winter, either trapped by the terrain or facing overwhelming odds, their strategies are: 1) Bury the weapons and scatter, waiting for an opportunity; 2) Falsely surrender and bide their time.

㈤ The Japanese Traitors' Method of Confiscating Weapons: Recently, they have become even more malicious. Those who surrender are repeatedly reorganized, and each reorganization results in numerous reductions, with the goal of collecting all the firearms scattered among the people.

㈥ The Pseudo-General Zhang Haipeng Seizes the Highest Military Authority in the Puppet State: Most of the important officials under him are his sons and nephews. The various regiments stationed in Jilin each have their own agendas. The concept of the nation and ethnicity is deeply rooted in them. Moreover, many of the smaller units of the Jilin righteous armies are defectors from his command. Whenever they are ordered to suppress our righteous armies, they often raise their rifles and shoot high, which is known as "shooting the friend's gun." What is most commendable is that his troops do not have a fixed number; our righteous armies can freely enter and leave, making it a haven for our righteous armies to escape. The recent sudden increase of tens of thousands of soldiers in Zhang's army illustrates this general situation.

㈦ The Entire Province of Jilin is in Utter Chaos: Last year, except for important cities and towns such as the provincial capital Changchun, our righteous armies occupied almost every other place. Under this sudden change and turmoil, order is extremely difficult to maintain; it can truly be called a living hell.

㈧ To this day, there is still unharvested grain in the counties of Jilin, left to feed cattle and livestock. Most of the houses and dwellings have been burned down. Old people, parents, wives, and children are scattered. Vitality is depleted. Famine is feared this year.

㈨ Under this sudden change, the general public, amid severe social terror, mostly lack a thorough understanding. They tend to believe it is a time of tribulation and fate. For a time, heresies are rampant. Such thoughts fill their empty minds, a truly pitiful situation.

㈩ In various religious rural villages, bankruptcy has reached an extreme. Initially, due to panic, people then sought various ways out. The fear of material life is irremediable, and spiritual comfort naturally arises. For a time, organizations such as the Big Sword Society, Yellow Sand Society, Red Spear Society, and Ruyi Sect are everywhere; there is no one without a society, no one without a sect. Chanting incantations and practicing vegetarianism, doctrines and Buddhist principles are spreading throughout the province.

A Tale of Blood and Tears from the Northeast 82

Report from Beiping: The loss of the Northeast has now been fifteen months. What is the internal situation in the Northeast now? Because the Japanese are covering things up and not revealing the truth, we have no way of knowing. I am now writing down what I have heard and seen, and report it to the nation.

(Factions within the Puppet State) 83

The puppet Manchurian state was created by the Japanese. Although it appears to be united, internally there are various factions. ㈠ The Restoration Faction: Led by Zheng Xiaoxu and supported by Puyi as its head. Although the Japanese are using Puyi to build the puppet state, Puyi also wants to use the puppet state as a stepping stone for restoration, to fulfill his imperial dreams. Zheng Xiaoxu has always been a key figure in the restoration plot, so he is naturally in cahoots with Puyi. However, the Japanese are quite suspicious of him. ㈠ The Concordia Association Faction: Jointly organized by Zhao Xinbo and others with the Japanese. Zhao and others have always been the most ardent pro-Japanese figures, so they organized this association with the Japanese, with the aim of promoting pro-Japanese sentiments and loyalty to the puppet state of Manchuria. Its mission is to promote the essence of the puppet state's founding and implement the Wangdao (Benevolent Rule) ideology. Japanese, Manchus, and Mongols can all freely join. The intention is nothing more than to curry favor with the Japanese and secure their positions and wealth. Therefore, the Japanese appear to be quite sympathetic to this faction. Like birds nesting on a dangerous curtain, not knowing what tomorrow brings, they are happily congratulating themselves, thinking they have succeeded. Living in a drunken dream, these puppets are the epitome of this.

(Anatomy of a Puppet) 84

Why are the Northeast puppets willing to act as puppets for the Japanese, enduring the scorn of the people without shame? Aside from a few who willingly betray the country, the rest are due to the following two reasons:

1. Since the September 18th Incident, ordinary unsuccessful figures in the opposition have all been recruited by the Japanese, given official titles, and promoted to serve as a rallying force. Since these people now have official positions, they temporarily ignore everything else. Those who crave official positions are also willing to be co-opted by the Japanese to seek temporary wealth.

2. Their personal lives and property are entirely in the hands of the Japanese. If they show the slightest dissent, the Japanese will confiscate their property on some pretext, and even their lives are not guaranteed. For the sake of their personal lives and property, the general public has no choice but to endure humiliation and accept the Japanese shackles.

In short, it is nothing more than a desire for temporary peace, and it is not a genuine willingness to work for the Japanese. Fortunately, the Japanese hold the power, and do not need the puppets to meddle too much. The Japanese see the puppets as nothing more than a kind of decoration. Therefore, these puppets only know to say yes and nod, doing nothing. They are officials in name only, in reality they are like straw men. As for ordinary lower-level civil and military officials, they are even more bored. These lower-level officials have no direct relationship with the Japanese, and there is no question of being pro-Japanese or anti-Japanese. They go to work and clock in every day, and receive their salaries on time every month, taking being an official as a profession and eating as a job. Other than that, there is nothing else. I once asked them why they did not go to Guannei (the area south of the Great Wall) to make a living. They replied that it was not easy to make a living in Guannei. Friends had gone to Beiping to wait for a job for half a year, and their funds had run out, but they still had not obtained a position. It was better to live in relative peace here, so they did not want to go to Guannei. From this, we can see that most of the officials in the puppet state are not really betraying the country, but are forced to endure humiliation for self-preservation.

(The Psychology of the People in the Northeast) 85

Although the Japanese have created a puppet state by pretending to represent the will of the people of the Northeast, the anti-Japanese sentiment of the people of the Northeast has not been submerged as a result. Observing the repeated efforts of the righteous armies in various places, braving the hail of bullets and fighting the Japanese with flesh and blood, we can know that the hearts of the people have not died, and there is a trend of becoming more and more激昂due to the Japanese oppression. For this reason, the Japanese are quite wary of the people of the Northeast. On the one hand, they use force to eliminate the righteous armies in various places, and on the other hand, they use their seductive tricks on the unarmed people in places like PanYang. They levy our national taxes, lend them to the farmers, and also summarily abolish one or two small miscellaneous taxes to ingratiate themselves with the general public. In the Shenyang area, theaters do not sell tickets, allowing villagers to enter and watch for free, and after watching, each person is given a bag of biscuits, hoping to use these small favors to buy out the entire anti-Japanese psychology of our people. However, if our people show the slightest anti-Japanese will, the disaster of death will immediately follow. Therefore, the people of the Northeast are well aware of this situation. The anti-Japanese sentiment is growing stronger and stronger. When the righteous armies approached Shenyang in mid-August of this year, the people were overjoyed, secretly congratulating each other, hoping that the righteous armies would come quickly and restore our homeland. Although the Japanese have tried every means to anesthetize the people, the people's hope for the government to recover the lost territories is even more urgent than that of the people in Guannei. The hearts of the people have not died. It all depends on our efforts. The country is not necessarily beyond saving.

(Glimpses of the Actions of the Japanese Army) 86

On the one hand, the Japanese are using various methods to seduce the people and eliminate their rebellious psychology. On the other hand, they are carrying out cruel massacres against those who are unyielding. We have already reported some of these facts in the newspapers. The usual abuse of the people is even too numerous to record. Here is a brief record of one or two:

(1) The people of the Northeast have completely lost their freedom of movement today. When walking on the road, if they encounter the Japanese army, they are often stopped and searched. If the villagers are slightly hesitant in their words due to fear, they are immediately branded as plotting something wrong and suspected of being anti-Japanese. They are not allowed to argue, and are even ordered to dig their own graves on the spot and be buried alive in them.

(2) The Japanese army frequently invades shops and residences at any time, arbitrarily searching. If any books promoting anti-Japanese sentiments and the Three Principles of the People, or printed with the words "Republic of China," are found, they are immediately branded as reactionary and arrested and imprisoned. The textbooks used in the various elementary schools have all been reviewed by the Japanese, and all nationalistic thoughts have been swept away. Zhongda University is almost unable to open.

(3) In the spring and summer of last year, the Japanese, under the pretext of epidemic prevention, forced people to inject vaccinations. After the injection, the skin at the injection site immediately bulged up and turned blue, taking a week to flatten.

(4) The Japanese army often uses the pretext of suppressing bandits to carry out massacres everywhere, often burning entire villages and towns to the ground, leaving no chickens or dogs alive. In fact, the bandits the Japanese call bandits are all our loyal and brave volunteer army. The Japanese are especially afraid of the volunteer army. Therefore, initially, the scope of the Japanese army's activities did not extend beyond the railway lines. Now, the strength of the volunteer army has been declining, and the footprints of the Japanese can be found in all the important towns and cities. The people of the Northeast have suffered greatly from the Japanese army's abuse. Those who are generally unarmed and unbrave are forced to commit suicide as a family, or to move their entire families to Guannei. The boats and vehicles are endless on the road, abandoning everything and leaving. Crying from hunger and cold, they are experiencing the extreme of human suffering. But this still refers to those who have some financial resources. The majority of poor people have no ability to escape, and can only allow the Japanese army to trample on them, or sell their sons and daughters to make travel expenses. The misery is even more unbearable to describe.

(The Views Held by Foreigners) 87

The newspapers and periodicals in the Northeast now are all monopolized by the Japanese. We who live there can never know the truth about the situation. The news about the righteous armies is even more strongly tabooed. What we can see are only one or two Western newspapers sent from outside. The Westerners who stay in the Northeast, with a little bit of fair judgment, are mostly dissatisfied with what the Japanese are doing. I once lived in the home of a Western friend, and they often mocked the Japanese as a form of entertainment. In their eyes, the Japanese are only worth one savage kind of person. But there are also those who speak for the Japanese. I once remembered a Western newspaper commentary saying that the Chinese national character is really a lazy nation. The methods adopted by the Japanese to deal with this kind of lazy nation are very proper. If these methods were transferred to any Western nation, there would probably be no peace for a single day. Although their words are absurd and outrageous, why are we being slandered to this point? Thinking about it, we can cry deeply. Fellow countrymen, for decades, we have been saying every day that the country is about to perish. Now the time of national demise has arrived. If we don't wake up now, it will be too late for regret. Please look at the people of the Northeast today. They are the example of our future. As I write this, my tears are already streaming down. Is China really beyond saving? Please see our future efforts. (January 3rd)

Guangdong Province's Three-Year Military Plan

Matters Concerning National Defense Have Been Announced 88

Report from Guangzhou: The Guangdong Provincial authorities have formulated a three-year governance plan. Regarding rectification, there are three items: officialdom, finance, and education. Regarding construction, there are four items: politics, economy, transportation, and education. Regarding military affairs, a three-year plan has also been drafted, which will be implemented starting on New Year's Day this year. The content of this plan, except for those not to be announced, includes the following excerpt from the section on national defense:

(Air Force) The first year's work includes: ㈠ All counties in the province purchase civilian aircraft and organize militia aviation; ㈡ Construct various aviation buildings; ㈢ Train aviation talent; ㈣ Increase the number of national defense aircraft squadrons; ㈤ Complete aircraft fields and aviation stations in all counties of the province, etc. In the second and third years, they will engage in training aircraft tactics and actively expanding combat aircraft, with a minimum target of over 150 aircraft, to consolidate air defense in South China. Regarding the economic aspect, in addition to promoting the sale of aviation prize bonds, they will find other ways to raise funds when necessary.

(Navy) In the first year, increase the number of river and sea defense warships by several tons, and strictly train the Marine Corps to become an elite force. In the second and third years, they will engage in purchasing artillery and machinery.

(Army) There will be no changes to the existing organizational structure. In the first year: ㈠ Save military expenses; ㈡ Eliminate inferior soldiers and retain the good ones in each unit to reduce the burden; ㈢ Improve training methods; ㈣ Rectify military preparations, etc. In the second and third years, they will engage in a policy of soldiers and farmers. As the local police teams are well-established, there is no need to station many troops in each county. When there is no war, the troops will be used for reclamation. When there is war, they will be transferred for national defense. The various Pacification Commissioner's offices have already begun planning model forestry centers, which is the first step in this plan. (January 3rd)

Guangdong Province Opposes the Establishment of Customs Branch Stations

Guangdong Provincial Government Orders All Customs Not to Establish Them 89

Pointing Out That It Conflicts with the Abolition of Likin Tax 90

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Ministry of Finance recently ordered the customs in Guangdong Province to establish more branch stations, and listed the names of the locations where branch stations and offices should be added, informing the Guangdong Provincial Government for its information. It is heard that after receiving the order, the Guangdong Provincial Government believed that it was difficult to implement the establishment of branch stations everywhere, and submitted it to the Southwest Political Affairs Conference for a resolution to not allow their establishment. The Provincial Government also issued a clear order to all Customs Superintendents yesterday, stating, "Upon review, the Provincial Government's 151st meeting of the Sixth Committee, proposed by the Chairman, holds that the original intent of the National Government's abolition of Likin tax was to develop domestic industry and commerce and to rectify national finances. Repeatedly, through three orders and five injunctions, all Likin taxes and all taxes similar to Likin throughout the country should be abolished, especially the customs stations that implement these harsh and detailed miscellaneous taxes should be closed, so as to avoid industry and commerce being restricted by excessive demands and delays, to alleviate their suffering, and to maintain the people's livelihood. The intention is excellent. As a result, the whole country has followed suit and the people have praised it. However, upon examining the Ministry of Finance's notice received on the 15th of this month, stating that according to the Inspector General of Customs, Mr. F.W. Maze's proposal for reorganizing the coastal branch stations of the Customs, the proposed branch stations and offices are appropriate for local conditions and convenient for control, and are considered feasible, and requesting a review, etc. Upon reviewing the attached list of various branch stations and offices, many are located inland, which seems to contradict the regulations for abolishing the fifty-mile regular customs within the abolition of Likin case. I am afraid that after implementation, it will be difficult to ensure that there will be no actions that harm the country and the people. Taking a step back, if the established branch stations and offices are not tax collection agencies, but only perform inspection duties, then their harassment can be predicted. Moreover, the Customs can only inspect at ports, but now they are encroaching on the interior, which is even more inappropriate. The reason for abolishing Likin taxes to benefit the people will instead incur popular resentment. The reason for alleviating the people's suffering will only increase the people's suffering. Although it is said that they are adapting to local conditions and convenient for control, such reversals will damage the nation's credibility, and national policies will fail. We must consider it carefully. It seems that we should reply to the Ministry of Finance and request cancellation, whether it is appropriate to wait for public decision and other words. While the discussion was ongoing, Lin Yizhong, Director of the Guangdong Department of Civil Affairs, presented a report stating, 'Your subordinate, the Director, this time, when inspecting the southern route, passed through Suixi County and the three customs branch stations of Mazhang, Chengyue, and Shentang along the county's highway. Because the county is adjacent to Chikan, and the highways are mostly connected to it, merchants transporting smuggled goods and evading taxes is common. Each of these branch stations, after 6:00 PM, must block the road at each station's location with wooden barriers. All passing vehicles must stop and wait for inspection. Their execution of duties, to prevent smuggling, seems to be appropriate. However, once the road is blocked, the vehicles that arrive must first pay a handling fee of three or four yuan before being released. Otherwise, they will use inspections as an excuse, delaying and obstructing them, even for dozens of minutes before they can pass. Even the daytime inspection procedures require the driver to personally enter the card officer's room to inquire and fill in who is riding in the car, how many people, etc., which takes at least fifteen minutes. This seems like an inspection that should be handled, but such harassment is no different from collecting road tolls, and it greatly hinders road traffic. Local people are complaining, and travelers and merchants are lamenting. The Director has witnessed this kind of malfeasance, harming merchants and the people, and cannot remain silent. It is appropriate to prepare a document and submit it to Your Excellency for review. I implore you to forward it to the Southwest Political Affairs Committee, ordering the Customs to instruct each of these branch stations to conduct inspections quickly in the future and not to collect fees, in order to eliminate the malfeasance and benefit transportation, etc.' Based on this, it was immediately submitted for review, and it was resolved to order the Customs Superintendents not to establish branch stations, and report it to the Southwest Political Affairs Committee for review, and inform the Ministry of Finance for its information, and separately inform the Pacification Commissioner's Offices in each district and the magistrates in each county. Apart from separately reporting for instructions, this order is hereby issued to your department for immediate notification, this order." (January 5th)

Preliminary Estimates of Major Crop Harvests in Jiangsu Province

Estimated by the Department of Agricultural Economics, College of Agriculture, Jinling University 91

In order to enable members of the public to understand the agricultural situation throughout the country, the Department of Agricultural Economics of the College of Agriculture of Jinling University began a pilot national agricultural survey and estimation in November 1932. This survey includes the harvest of major agricultural products in each province and the prosperity or decline of the rural economy in various places. To date, more than 1,000 reports have been received from various provinces. Based on the information from 129 reports from 41 counties in Jiangsu Province, the following preliminary estimates are made:

Since the YuGuan Incident, the arrogance of the Japanese has been rampant, but there is nothing that can be done about it. Suzhou

Robbery Outside Changmen Gate in the Early Morning 93

At 8:00 AM yesterday (10th), four robbers suddenly arrived at the Fulaide Electrical Materials Store on Damalu Road outside Changmen Gate, each carrying a handgun. At that time, the iron gate of the store was already open, but the wooden doors had not been fully opened. The four robbers forced a clerk who had gotten up to return upstairs and awakened the eleven employees who had not yet gotten up, driving them into the warehouse. One robber guarded them while the remaining robbers searched the store once. They then opened the iron box, robbing 141 silver dollars and 458 dimes. Finally, they returned to the upstairs and searched each employee's bedroom bedside before locking the warehouse, locking everyone inside, and leaving leisurely.

Suspicious Homicide Case Occurs Inside Changmen 94

A suspicious homicide case occurred inside the Chengtian Temple Grand Ironworks Alley in Changmen, Suzhou City. The detailed records are as follows: The case occurred at Wang Jinji Tailor Shop, No. 23 Grand Ironworks Alley. The shop owner, Wang Jingui, is from Zhutang, Jiangyin. He has four brothers. The youngest brother, named Zenggui, is 30 years old. He has been a partner at Xintai Qianzhuang on Hulong Street for 16 years. Four years ago, Zenggui brought his wife, née Fei (29 years old), a son, and a daughter to Suzhou to live with his brother Jingui. Zenggui would return to the Ironworks Alley at night to live with his wife, but sometimes he would stay at the Xintai shop. Zenggui’s room was upstairs facing the street, and there was a small toilet under the wall. Wang Jinji had a partner named Alin, 28 years old, from Changrehongta. He had been a partner in the shop for seven years. This past June, née Fei was cooling off at the back gate of Chengtian Temple when Alin began to flirt with her. On the night of July 18, when Zenggui was staying at the Xintai shop, Alin sneaked into née Fei’s room and had secret relations with her. However, Jingui heard the noise and investigated. The next day, they negotiated at the Yitu Teahouse. In the end, Zenggui wanted to divorce his wife and asked Alin to pay 300 yuan to take née Fei. Alin returned to his hometown to raise the money. When he came to Suzhou with the money, Zenggui suddenly regretted his decision. Jingui also fired Alin. After that, Alin lingered on the street corner, constantly enticing née Fei to elope with him from the front and back doors of Wang Jinji’s shop. Née Fei told Zenggui, who instructed her not to go out. From this month onwards, née Fei stayed upstairs with the door closed, not taking a single step outside. Suddenly, on the morning of the 9th at 9:00 AM, Zenggui went to Jiangyin to collect debts. At 2:00 AM that night, Alin braved the rain and climbed from the toilet outside the wall into née Fei’s room, took off his clothes, got into bed, and crawled under the covers. Née Fei woke up in shock. She was in a difficult situation and could hardly resist. At that time, Alin immediately told née Fei that even though they were far apart, he would always think of her. He was determined to elope with her today. If the doors were heavily guarded, they could go through the roof. Otherwise, he had a sharp blade today and was willing to die together with her. When née Fei heard about the knife, she shouted "No!" Wang Jingui and others heard the alarm and went upstairs, where they saw Alin lying naked in a pool of blood. A razor was inserted horizontally into his neck. He had already committed suicide. It was 3:00 AM. They immediately reported to the police. Alin was already dead. After the case occurred, viewers gathered and there was much discussion. Everyone doubted the suicide. At 5:00 PM on the afternoon of the 10th, after the court's examination, the wound was deeper on the left and shallower on the right, and his right hand was curved, so it was determined to be a suicide.

Wuxi

Petition to Maintain Agricultural and Sericultural Organizations 95

The Wuxi Sericulture Control Office and the Jiangdu Original Silkworm Seed Manufacturing Factory have achieved remarkable results since their establishment and are the foundation for fundamentally improving the silkworm industry by implementing silkworm seed restrictions. The Department of Industry, after discussion with the provincial government, decided to abolish them. All affiliated organizations were also to be closed by the end of the year and handed over to the Department of Construction for safekeeping. The leaders of the silk and silkworm industry in Jiangsu Province have submitted petitions to the central and provincial governments, requesting that the above two organizations be maintained and not closed down. Recently, the silk and silkworm industry in Jiangsu Province and Zheng Bijiang, Shao Shenpei, Lu Zirong, Fei Kuisheng, Xue Shouxuan, Qian Fenghao, Gu Shuzhi, Gao Jiansi, and others who are related to the agricultural, sericultural, and silk businesses in Wuxi City have held a meeting. They all agreed that Jiangsu Province is an agricultural area for silkworms and mulberries, and now is the time to improve sericulture and promote agricultural products. Organizations that have been established and have achieved results, such as the Jiangdu Original Silkworm Seed Manufacturing Factory, the Wuxi Sericulture Control Office, and the Wuxi Silk and Agricultural Farm, especially those with outstanding achievements, should not only be maintained as usual, but also be promoted as much as possible in order to improve the silk industry in Jiangsu Province and alleviate the economic situation of farmers. It was decided to jointly send a telegram to the province, requesting maintenance, and to appoint Gao Jiansi, Qian Fenghao, and Xue Shouxuan as representatives to go to Zhenjiang to petition the provincial government. The three representatives, Gao, Qian, and Xue, went to the province yesterday (the 10th) morning.

Continuous Occurrences of Robbery Cases in Rural Areas 96

Li Afu, a resident of Shandun Lane, Zhuji Township, Second District of the county, is engaged in farming. At 6:30 PM the night before last, three robbers dressed in black and wearing felt hats, each armed with a pistol, broke into Li's house and ordered the owner to stop. They searched everywhere and robbed eleven pieces of cotton clothing and four pieces of gold jewelry. After the robbers got the loot, they went to rob the Zhang Shenglin family next door. However, it was still early, and the neighbors were already prepared, so as soon as they entered Zhang's house, the gongs outside began to sound. The robbers fired three shots and fled. Also, the house of Xue Jinhe, a villager in Wujing Bridge, Longshan Township, was broken into by three or four robbers around 2:00 AM the day before yesterday. The robbers broke down the door and tied up the owner, arbitrarily searching for loot. Jinhe's younger brother, Sanbao, escaped and sounded the alarm. The robbers set off two firecrackers and fled with the loot. By the time the police from the Ninth Sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau arrived, the robbers were long gone.

Zhenjiang

Progress of the Sujia Road Project 97

The Sujia Road starts from Suzhou and ends in Jiaxing, Zhejiang. The section within Jiangsu Province has been under construction since the Jiangsu Construction Department established an engineering office in September last year. The progress of the project has been rapid. The section between Suzhou and Wujiang has been completely completed, and the road surface is new and very smooth. Vehicles can now pass through. The old Baodai Bridge in this section has long been famous in Suzhou. This time, during the construction of the road, a new bridge was built next to the old bridge, named New Baodai Bridge. The bridge is over 800 feet long and is the longest in Jiangsu Province. The bridge was completed at the end of the lunar year. The earthwork for the section from Wujiang to the Zhejiang border has also been completed. A total of 47 bridges have been built, about 30 of which have been completed. The road surface project in this section, with newly built earthwork that is not yet solid, is said to require further work after the roadbed is firm after rain and snow. The entire project is expected to be fully completed by the end of March this year. The Jiangsu Construction Department is currently planning to establish a long-distance bus service on the road and has been in contact with manufacturers in Shanghai to order vehicles. The planned equipment is quite complete. In the future, travel between Suzhou and Jiaxing should be comfortable and convenient. The Sujia Road is about 75 kilometers long, about 60 kilometers of which are in Jiangsu. The cost of the Jiangsu section is said to be about 550,000 yuan.

Canal Works Bureau Opens River Barriers 98

The Jiangbei Canal Works Bureau previously built river barriers during the post-disaster reconstruction works of each section. These barriers blocked commercial transportation. Various trade associations have repeatedly sent letters and telegrams requesting that they be opened. Now that the works in areas such as Lai Sheng'an have been completed one after another, the bureau has sent engineer Zhang Longchuan, together with Tao Pei, a river official from Jiangdu, to lead a team of supervisors and soldiers to open the river barriers of each section. The work should be completed on the 10th to facilitate commercial transportation.

Hangzhou

Bandit Wu Zhiqing Executed by Firing Squad 100

The provincial government, based on the report from the Third Regiment of the Security Team, determined that a soldier named Wu Zhiqing was actually named Wu Zhangfa. In 1920, in his hometown of Yiwu, he joined with convicted criminals Yu Xunmao, Shen Huangzhao, Chen Zhengcai, Ruan Qishu, and others to kidnap Shen Zhirun, Yu Xunping, Sheng Zhangsong, Wang Jingyu, Wu Chengyao, Pan Weixing, and others, demanding ransom money. In July of the same year, the bandit leader Hu Piqiu and others went to Hongtangban, Jinhua, to carry out a robbery. The bandit leader Hu Piqiu was killed on the spot by the people. His wife then led more than a hundred bandits to burn down all the houses in the village. The criminal Wu Zhangfa also participated in the scene. He had been wanted by the military and police for a long time without being caught. The criminal fled outside, changed his name to Wu Zhiqing, and enlisted in the 12th Company of the 4th Battalion of the Third Regiment of the Security Team. The Security Regiment of the Third District of Yiwu County learned about this, reported it to the county, which in turn reported it to the government, ordering the regiment to detain the criminal soldier and bring him to the province. The victims were summoned to the court for questioning, and the facts were clarified. He was sentenced to death. On the morning of the 10th of this month at 8:00 AM, the criminal Wu Zhiqing, alias Wu Zhangfa, was identified, bound, and taken outside Qingbo Gate to be executed by firing squad.

Page 9

Li Liejun Advocates for Active Armed Resistance Against Japan 101

Feng Yuxiang sent a telegram to Li and others the day before yesterday, saying that compromise with Japan is the enemy.

The North China issue is becoming more and more serious. Our reporter interviewed Li Liejun, a member of the Central Committee staying in Shanghai, yesterday and asked for his opinion on the national affairs. According to Li, their political views have been expressed repeatedly, that is, advocating active armed resistance against foreign aggression and promoting the realization of democracy at home. After the Yu Incident, the ambitions of the Japanese warlords became more and more exposed to the world. For us, we can only implement the doctrine of armed resistance against Japan. To sit and wait for death is better than fighting to the death. Otherwise, if we let them slaughter us, the country will be destroyed in no time. The reporter then asked if Feng Yuxiang had sent any recent telegrams. Li replied that Mr. Feng is enthusiastically patriotic. Since hearing about the Yu Incident, he has been filled with righteous indignation and has repeatedly expressed his willingness to join the volunteer army to kill the enemy. Yesterday (the day before yesterday), he sent another telegram to Li and Mr. Xu Jilong, stating his advocacy of armed resistance against Japan, saying that those who carry out or support resistance against Japan are our friends, and those who compromise with Japan are our enemies. His agitation and indignation can be seen. Finally, Feng advocated forming an anti-Japanese fundraising association in Shanghai to prepare for logistics and other aspects.

Feng Zhanhai's Representative Pang Yuedong Discusses the Course of the Anti-Japanese War 103

Bitterly fought for years, retreated from Rehe

Now has an elite force of 40,000 men

General Feng Zhanhai, commander-in-chief of the 9th Army of the Northeast Volunteer Army, led his troops in fighting for more than a year between Changchun and Harbin in Jilin, repeatedly capturing famous cities and once recovering and besieging Harbin, a major city in the Northeast, threatening the Japanese invaders and their puppet regime. Due to lack of ammunition and supplies, he retreated to the border of Rehe. Recently, he sent his chief of staff, Pang Yuedong, as a representative to Shanghai to report on the war and request assistance. A reporter from the New Voice News Agency visited Pang at his residence yesterday and talked in detail about the anti-Japanese war of Feng's troops and their current situation.

Beginning of the Anti-Japanese War: Feng Zhanhai was originally the commander of the guard regiment of Zhang Zuoxiang's department in Jilin, with three battalions of infantry, one battalion of cavalry, one battalion of mountain artillery, and one company each of mortars and machine guns. Each infantry battalion had eight light machine guns, so the equipment was quite complete and relatively new. When the September 18th Incident occurred, when the Northeast armies were ordered to retreat, the chief of the Jilin government, Xi Qia, a traitor, took full power as chief of staff and ordered Feng to lead his troops lightly out of the province. The so-called lightly armed meant that they only carried guns and no bullets. Feng eventually took out all the mountain artillery shells, etc., and led a battalion of engineers to retreat to Panshi County, south of Jilin Province. At that time, although the true situation of the situation was not clear, he was already preparing to concentrate military power for resistance. Later, he fought around Acheng, Shuangcheng, Yushu, and other places along the Harbin-Changchun Railway. Soldiers and civilians from Jilin Province came to join him, and at most the number of his troops reached 140,000. Later, because of the complexity of the composition, and some who did not abide by military discipline, he was reorganized to 110,000.

Ammunition Replenishment: Feng's army fought around the Harbin-Changchun Line for more than a year. Because the soldiers had no radio station, they could not transmit the war situation at any time. Therefore, they did not receive any assistance from compatriots at home and abroad. The local people were also happy to transport the troops' supplies. The righteous soldiers gave their lives for the country and endured hardship as if it were sweetness. The most difficult thing was the replenishment of ammunition. However, the reason why they were able to persist for more than a year was that Feng had carried a lot of ammunition when he left the provincial capital. Later, the Japanese invaders instigated the puppet state to organize five bandit suppression brigades to fight against the righteous army. As a result, most of the soldiers of these five brigades brought their weapons and came back, and they got a lot of ammunition. Moreover, there were many civilian armed forces in the Northeast, and wealthy families often hid tens of thousands of bullets. Feng's army fought for several months and was trusted by the local people, so many enthusiastically transported them. As a result, they captured Wuchang, Yushu, Shuangcheng, Acheng, Fangzheng, Baoxian (formerly Weizigou), Yanshou (formerly Tongshi), Zhuhe, Shulan, Detonghui, and other counties, and once recovered Harbin and Jilin twice, besieging Harbin, making the Japanese invaders and their puppet regime uneasy. Rehe After fighting to the end, in July and August of last year, because the ammunition was gradually lacking, and the uniforms of the troops were very thin, and the north was cold early, and the winter was approaching, the righteous soldiers still had no cotton clothes, so they led 40,000 elites across the tributary of the Songhua River from Shulan, passing through Dehui, Nong'an (that is, the former Huanglong Prefecture in the west of the Harbin-Changchun Line), Changling, Kaitong (on the Siping-Taonan Road), Zhanyu, and reaching Kailu, Rehe. There are still more than 40,000 people left in the eastern part of Jilin Province, under the command of Wang Rongwu. By order of Feng Zhanhai, they are breaking up into pieces and carrying out harassment in the Jilin-Changchun Road area to destroy the facilities of the puppet regime.

Donations Received: Donations from all over the country to support the righteous army amounted to more than one million. Feng's troops in Jilin had no access. After reaching the border of Rehe, General Zhu Ziqiao gave them 80,000 yuan. As for cotton clothes and cold clothes, they have only recently been given access, and many have frozen to death. It was also heard from Liu Pixian, the representative of Li Du, that the two departments of Li Du and Ding Chao received a total of 70,000 yuan in donations from Shanghai. Combining the four departments of Ding Li Feng Wang (Delin), the total amount of donations received by the righteous army officially fighting in the Eastern Province is less than 300,000 yuan.

Now they are holding on to the Dachanzi Dazigou area for reorganization and replenishment, waiting for an opportunity to counterattack. The morale is extremely high. ㈡ More than 4,000 old troops recruited by me in Qingyun Yanshan are gathering to set off and work together to save the country. ㈢ The righteous armies in Jin and Rehe suffered six or seven casualties in this battle. Huang Naishu Talks About Yucheng Post Office

Unwilling to Give Up Unless Absolutely Necessary 106

Central News Agency reported that Huang Naishu, director of the Shanghai Postal Administration, told the Central News Agency reporter that the mail in Yucheng is still being delivered as usual. At the beginning of the incident, because the news was blocked and the true situation was unknown, the mail was not stopped. Later, after receiving the bad news of the fall of the city and the interruption of railway traffic, the mail in that area was stopped. On the one hand, efforts were made to maintain postal operations. Fortunately, although the situation in Qinhuangdao was urgent, the railway traffic had not been interrupted. Therefore, all the mail in Yucheng was transported to Qinhuangdao by rail, and then transferred to the couriers on foot. The distance between the two places is about 20 miles, and it takes a long time to deliver on foot, but it is not too late. At the same time, the Yucheng Post Office reported that the local order was very chaotic, so the original number of branch offices were merged into one office, and all the employees were able to endure the difficulties and work with peace of mind. Therefore, unless something unexpected happens in Qinhuangdao, the postal operation will not be interrupted, and the Yucheng Post Office is unwilling to give up the postal rights unless it is absolutely necessary.

The Bank Note Exchange Officially Opened Yesterday 107

Two exchanges in the morning and afternoon achieved excellent results

A committee was established to appoint supervisors and instructors

The Note Exchange jointly operated by the United Preparation Committee of the Shanghai Banking Association officially opened yesterday. First, head silver dollars were exchanged. The first exchange was at 11:00 AM, and the second exchange was at 3:20 PM. A committee was established to appoint supervisors and instructors. The details are as follows:

(Official Exchange) The Note Exchange officially opened yesterday without holding any ceremony. Starting at 9:00 AM, many Chinese and foreign people went to congratulate and visit, and were received by Manager Zhu Puquan and others. By 10:50 AM, all the exchange members of the exchange banks had arrived. At 11:05 AM, Manager Zhu Puquan rang the bell to implement the first exchange. After submitting the first report form, the note notification was transferred according to the number, and then the second report form was submitted. The chief clearing officer reported the difference, and finally the difference transfer statement and the duplicate notification form were filled out and submitted. It was completed at 11:29 AM. The originally scheduled time was 30 minutes. Because the exchange members were very proficient after the trial, it only took 24 minutes to complete.

(Establishment of the Committee) According to the resolution of the sixth committee representative meeting on November 19, 1921, a Note Exchange Committee was established. In addition to Manager Zhu Puquan as a member, there were nine members to handle the design of all affairs of the exchange and the matters of establishing various rules. It was also decided at the first gold meeting of the committee to elect three members from the Bank of China, Cheng Muhao, the Bank of Communications, Qian Lugin, and the Shanghai Bank, Yang Liumei, as supervisors and instructors. The address of the committee is attached to the United Preparation Committee of the Banking Association.

Various Trade Groups Fight for Telephone Price Increase

Yesterday's Letter to the Shanghai Municipal Council 109

Various trade associations in this city, regarding the matter of increased telephone rates in the concessions, have not yet reached a satisfactory resolution. Therefore, yesterday a special letter was sent to the Shanghai Municipal Council, requesting reconsideration, in order to resolve the situation as soon as possible. The original letter, jointly signed and sealed by over thirty trade associations, is as follows: "To the esteemed Shanghai Municipal Council, regarding the matter of increased telephone rates, our associations, based on the demands of users, unanimously and firmly oppose it. However, prolonged stalemate is not beneficial to the concessions. We hereby propose to your Council the following key points: (1) Although the news of the telephone rate increase was disclosed in Chinese newspapers in July, there was absolutely no prior announcement of the implementation measures. Moreover, the company requires users to retroactively compensate for the new rates, which has never happened before and is unreasonable and unlawful. Furthermore, non-retroactivity is a universally recognized legal principle. Now, Mr. Jones, the Secretary-General of your Council, tolerates the retroactive increase starting from March 27th, which seems to show bias towards the company. We believe that Mr. Jones, the Secretary-General of your Council, was originally a lawyer, how could he not know this? Knowing but not speaking, causing this mistake, we request your Council to quickly correct this error and rectify it. (2) The Shanghai Municipal Gazette of October 21st published Mr. Anson's letter to Mr. Jones, the Secretary-General of your Council, regarding opinions on the telephone rate increase. Upon investigation, the meaning of the third paragraph of that letter admits that this opinion did not consider the economic changes during this period. It also stated that if he were asked to come to China again for investigation, he would surely provide another report to satisfy our hopes. This proves that Mr. Anson's previous report admitted that it could not consider the interests of the majority of the public, leading to disputes. Therefore, the price increase has lost its basis. (3) The Shanghai Telephone Company incurred huge expenses due to the replacement of new equipment and expansion of lines. According to its own statement, from the company's establishment on August 5, 1930, to the end of September this year, a period of 26 months, the cost increased to a huge sum of 28 million taels due to the replacement of automatic equipment and expansion of new facilities, resulting in a total loss of 218,430 taels. Considering the loss over 26 months, the company has strived to expand its lines more than fourfold, and most of its staff are Westerners with high salaries. The loss due to extravagance and miscalculation is a natural consequence and cannot be used as a sufficient reason for a huge price increase and retroactive compensation for new prices. For the present plan, if you want to eliminate disputes and quell the storm, the only way is to have an impartial social organization recommend an accounting expert to audit the company's accounts to determine whether the price increase is unavoidable and whether the amount of the increase is appropriate, in order to seek a fair solution. We have always admired the gentlemen of your Council as enlightened individuals with fair judgment. This humble suggestion is respectfully submitted for inclusion on the agenda and a prompt vote to appease the expectations of the public. In addition to submitting the original letter with the joint signatures and seals of our associations to your Council, we are also sending a copy to your Council for reference and hope for your sympathy and permission to propose the motion for discussion. Respectfully addressed to the Gentlemen of the Shanghai Municipal Council of the Shanghai International Settlement." Followed by a list of organizations: Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Association, Shanghai General Association of Commercial Circles, Shanghai Special District Telephone Users' Association, Shanghai Citizens' First District Branch, Nanjing Road Commercial Circles Association, Shanghai Citizens' Eighth District Branch, Joint Office of the Shanghai Citizens' Hongkou Broadway District Branch, Henan Road Commercial Circles Association, Shanghai Embroidery Trade Association, Shanghai Citizens' Twentieth District Branch, Shanghai Citizens' Twenty-fourth District Branch, Shanghai Biscuit, Candy, and Canned Food Trade Association, Sima Road Commercial Circles Association, Shanghai Citizens' Fifth District Branch, Shanghai Knitting Trade Association, Shanghai Citizens' Twenty-seventh District Branch, Shanghai Department Store Trade Association, Shanghai Citizens' Tenth District Branch, Chaozhou Association in Shanghai, Hongkou Sixth Road Commercial Circles Association, Shanghai Citizens' Twenty-second District Branch, Shanghai Citizens' Eighteenth District Branch, Shanghai Citizens' Seventh District Branch, Shanghai Citizens' Sixth District Branch, Broadway Road Commercial Circles Association, Xihua Road Commercial Circles Association, Shanghai Citizens' Fifteenth District Branch, Suzhou Road Commercial Circles Association, Shanghai Citizens' Twelfth District Branch, Shanghai Citizens' Fourteenth District Branch, Shanghai Citizens' Eleventh District Branch, Wuma Road Commercial Circles Association, Shanghai Towel Trade Association.

Shanghai-Ping Air Service Inaugurated Yesterday Morning 116

But Returned Twice Due to Fog

Rescheduled to Fly Again This Morning

The Shanghai-Ping air route of China National Aviation Corporation was originally scheduled to take off from Shanghai at 7:30 AM yesterday morning. However, due to heavy fog yesterday morning, it was delayed until 11:05 AM before taking off. However, it returned twice due to fog en route. Details are as follows:

=Returned Twice= After the heavy rain stopped yesterday morning, heavy fog filled the sky. The Shanghai-Ping route's "Bengbu" aircraft was delayed until 11:05 AM when the heavy fog subsided slightly before taking off, piloted by foreign pilot An Lishang. Nie Kaiyi, the director of the company, traveled with him, carrying 783 kilograms of airmail. It flew along the Yangtze River towards Nanjing. However, before flying for 15 minutes, dense fog reappeared, so it turned to land near the Zhenru Radio Station. At 11:45 AM, when the dense fog subsided slightly, it took off for the second time. However, it was still blocked by fog en route and returned to Longhua Airport at 12:05 PM.

=Continued Flight This Morning= After the aircraft returned to Longhua, Director Nie Kaiyi immediately telegraphed the Shanghai General Manager to report the experience of being blocked and returning, briefly stating, "We flew north at 11:10 AM, but were immediately blocked by fog and landed near the Zhenru Radio Station. At 11:45 AM, the weather cleared and the dense fog subsided slightly, so we took off for the second time. However, we were blocked by fog en route and returned to Longhua at 12:05 PM." Yesterday, Li Diezhuang, the secretary of the company, told a reporter from the Central News Agency that yesterday's (i.e., yesterday) test flight was turned back due to fog and rescheduled to fly again at 7:30 AM tomorrow morning (i.e., this morning).

=Shanghai-Hankou Also Blocked= The company's Shanghai-Hankou westbound aircraft was also delayed until 10:45 AM due to fog yesterday morning. It was also blocked by fog en route and returned at 12:10 PM. The aircraft flying from Hankou to Shanghai was also blocked by fog.

The China Merchants "Jiangda" Steamship Has Been Freed from Danger 118

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's "Jiangda" steamship, which operates along the Yangtze River, set out from Hankou. About ten miles downstream of Hankou, on the Yutao River surface, it suddenly ran aground due to shallow water in winter. The "Jiangda" immediately sent a wireless message to notify the Hankou branch for rescue. At that time, the "Xingshi" and "Liji" happened to be in Hankou, so they sailed out to rescue. They pulled the "Jiangda" out of danger. Fortunately, it was in a shallow beach, and there was no major loss. According to Zhao Yuntai, the director of the shipping department of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, he received a report that the "Jiangda" steamship had been safely rescued.

Case of Encirclement and Land Acquisition in Pengpu

Municipal Government Sends Representatives to Participate in Ministry Meeting 119

Nanjing Electric: Regarding the case of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Bureau encircling and acquiring private land in the Pengpu area of Shanghai to build a joint transportation station, the landowners in the area have repeatedly appealed to the central authorities to avoid it. The Executive Yuan has decided to hand it over to the Ministry of Interior, together with the Ministry of Railways and the Ministry of Military Affairs, for consultation. The Shanghai Municipal Government has also requested to participate. The Ministry has decided to convene a meeting on the afternoon of the 11th. The Ministry and the Shanghai Municipal Government have designated representatives to participate.
