Hangzhou Elementary School Teachers Take Collective Leave

City Government Responds by Paying Overdue Fees 159

Due to the provincial government's order to tighten the city government's operating expenses, all elementary school teachers in Hangzhou took collective leave. Mayor Zhao Zhihao, citing the difficulty of municipal development, firmly requested the withdrawal of the order and fought for it with his resignation. As a result, the salaries of elementary school teachers in the city for December of last year have not yet been paid, and the salaries for this month and the two installments of seniority pay are even more uncertain. All elementary school teachers, due to the lack of guarantee for their living expenses, had long intended to take collective leave as a passive resistance. After several consultations with the city government's education authorities, it was decided that the December educational expenses and the last seniority payment would be verified and issued separately on the 14th and 15th of this month. However, there is no definite date for the payment of this month's salary and the next seniority payment, and there are still discounts. Therefore, on the afternoon of the 9th, they took collective leave and convened more than 400 elementary school teachers in the Yousheng Guanxiang Elementary School to discuss countermeasures. They requested that the salaries for December and January and the two semesters of seniority pay be paid before the winter vacation, that the discounts be cancelled, and that the elementary school funding be independent. Tang Gensheng, He Jingwu, and four others were elected as general representatives to lead all the teachers to petition the city government. Mayor Zhao personally replied that 1) discounts would be eliminated and monthly salaries would be paid on time; 2) the unpaid part of the last seniority payment would be paid before the winter vacation within a possible range; 3) the regular expenses for December 1932 would be paid on January 14, and half of this month's expenses would be paid first.

Jiangning Elementary School Fee Arrears Dispute

▲ Jiangning Education on the Verge of Bankruptcy 160

▲ Financial Authorities Urged to Seek Reform Quickly 161

Jiangning elementary school education funds, because the financial authorities have historically been economically opaque, and the education bureau receives a varying amount of money each month from the financial bureau, which it has no power over and lacks independence. The fees for October 1931 are already four or five months behind, and then water disasters and national crises followed, and the financial bureau took this excuse to pay less educational funds. The money collected by Jiangning Educational funds through financial bureau on behalf of the district is 190,000 yuan per year, but the financial bureau sends only one or two thousand to the educational bureau per month. Even during festivals when more is allocated, the amount is only four or five thousand yuan. It is said that a former finance bureau chief paid the education bureau only a few hundred yuan per month when he was about to hand over the position, causing the education bureau to owe the primary schools more than ten months' worth of funds. The root cause of the arrears is that the peasants of Jiangning County do not pay their taxes directly to the financial bureau, but they are collected by the tax collectors on behalf of the bureau, and less is reported, though the county has a quota. However, the financial bureau failed to seriously address the situation, and the problem of embezzlement is more than enough. Overall it is said that the farmers cannot pay the tax, and sometimes when they do come up with the money, they say it is borrowed, which is nominally 'borrowed' but not collected. Ever since Chairman Chiang heard that Jiangning Educational fees were too far behind and were unsustainable, he summoned the heads of the financial and educational bureaus and asked them about the situation. On December 15, half a month of elementary school expenses were issued, and at the end of December, another month's expenses were issued. But the pain was too deep. Even though Chairman Chiang Kai-shek gave a shot of morphine, it only provided temporary relief and was not a permanent solution. It was recently heard that the Jiangning County Finance Bureau Director was taken over by County Chief Zhao, who expressed his active desire to sort things out and eliminate corruption and strictly fix the tax collection quota with tax collectors and enforce a collection policy instead of borrowing. Hopefully, the County Chief will earnestly handle matters and never again allow education in Jiangning county to fall into bankruptcy. It was also heard that Jiangning County elementary school teachers recently hosted newspaper reporters to report the details of the fees that were owed to them, and that some schools have already run out of food. It is hoped that the media will provide support.

After the Shandong Student Protest Was Resolved, the Senior High Schools Resumed Classes

Students Are Allowed to Attend Classes Starting on the 21st After Being Screened 162

Jinan Fast News: High school students in Shandong Province opposed old conferences, went on strike and boycotted class, and affected students from other schools such as Yizhong Zheng Yi, Ai Mei, Qi Lu, Zhen Hua and other eight schools. After the joint strike and petition, eight schools, including Yizhong, followed the orders of the Education Department and resumed classes separately. However, the senior high school students did not listen to the advice, so they had no choice but to disband them and order the students to leave the school and return to their hometowns to await screening. It is now heard that the middle school has followed the order of the Education Department and notified the parents of students in the first and second grades of the general course and the students in the third year of the liberal arts course and the lower grades of the science course, except for a few students who took the most initiative, who will be severely punished separately, and required each student to fill in the guarantee form and pay the fees from today (7th) to the 11th, and then move into the school to wait for screening. It is also heard that the students in the liberal arts and science courses in the third year and the lower grades of the science course had previously requested to be exempted from the exam, and then all withdrew from school. Most of the students had received withdrawal certificates, and a few students left without receiving them. Now most of the students have repented and jointly submitted a report to the school authorities, requesting to graduate and join the exam. The school authorities, considering the situation of each student, have submitted a report to the Education Department, and although they have received withdrawal certificates, they should be allowed to graduate to the 45 who the school deems fulfill their criteria. The school also held a graduation exam on the 6th. After the results of the exam are announced, it will be submitted to the Education Department for a graduation exam. According to He Siyuan, the head of the Education Department, although the students in the third year of the liberal arts and science courses who should have graduated from the winter vacation had previously withdrawn from school and received withdrawal certificates, some of them did not receive them, so the school allowed them to graduate in accordance with the regulations. The report came to the department, and those who took the initiative to withdraw during the turmoil were not allowed to submit repentance letters, while those who did not withdraw at the time were allowed to graduate. A total of 45 people were counted. The exam was held yesterday.

According to the person in charge of the school, the graduation exam of our school will be announced on the 9th, and those who pass will be sent to the Education Department for the joint exam. As for the students in the first and second grades and the upper grades of the third year of the school, they have been notified to fill in the guarantee forms and conduct a strict screening. The school is scheduled to hold the screening period from the 12th to the 15th of this month, and the class can start on the 18th. But at most it cannot be extended past the 20th. It is now heard that as of today (7th), more than 60 students have filled in the guarantee forms and paid fees to enter the school.

High School Curriculum Standards (5) 163

(4) In addition to lecturing on the regular curriculum, if there is extra time, supplementary teaching materials may be added in the classroom. However, students should be instructed to practice their note-taking skills, organize them neatly, and submit them to the teacher for evaluation. It is not advisable to compile lecture notes and distribute them to students.

(II) Key Teaching Points

(1) General Remarks: High school teaching materials are the second circumference of junior high school teaching materials, so there should be a real connection with the former.

(1) The earliest part of high school mathematics is the same as the junior high school teaching materials. It is advisable to select more difficult problems for review and to introduce deeper research.

(2) Junior high school mathematics focuses on the proficiency of calculation skills and the understanding of basic concepts. The research method is to summarize from examples and special cases into general rules. High school should focus on theoretical aspects, using deductive methods for more systematic research. Due to the complexity and depth of mathematical principles, junior high school students may not be able to fully understand them. Therefore, high school should reiterate the junior high school teaching materials, but with different levels of detail and different focuses, so that students will not be bored, and there will be a sense of reviewing the old and knowing the new, peeling cocoons and drawing silk.

(3) The high school mathematics subject only has twenty class hours, and there are as many as five or six compulsory courses. Instead of teaching too much material in detail and having students memorize it, it is better to focus on basic training and cultivate their ability to conduct research independently. Therefore, for solid geometry, higher algebra, and analytic geometry, only the main ideas need to be taught, but attention should be drawn when problems cannot be thoroughly explored to inspire students' ambition to pursue higher research.

(2) Algebra and Higher Algebra: High school algebra should focus on functions and equations.

(1) Students do not easily understand the concept of functions. Teachers should pay attention to explaining when deriving the variable values and signs of elementary functions in order to establish their foundation. The quadratic function is the most suitable example.

(2) Junior high school graduates can already understand the solutions of equations, so high school algebra should focus on the general properties of equations, the principle of equivalent solutions, and discussion of changes in solutions ("equations containing parameters") and increases or decreases ("such as the roots of fractional equations and irrational equations"). Quadratic equations are the gateway to equations and are most sufficient to train students' thinking.

(3) Higher algebra takes the theory of equations as the center. The existence of complex numbers is a prerequisite for the establishment of basic algebraic theorems. Determinants are a powerful tool for elimination. Although series are extreme operations and differ greatly from algebraic properties, all function expansions rely on them and are the basis of analytic geometry, so more attention should be paid to them.

(4) The application problems of equations are not only limited to daily facts but should also be linked to geometry, trigonometry, physics, and chemistry. The accuracy of the results obtained should be noted in practical problems. The numerical solution of high-order numerical equations has much practical use and should be known by those who study calculation. Probability is the core of statistics and should also be taught in general terms.

(3) Geometry: High school geometry should train students' ability to explore automatically and pay attention to the logical order so that they reach a considerable degree of rigor.

(1) Geometry places the greatest emphasis on logical order. Junior high school students are young and not easy to strictly adhere to it. High school geometry teaching should pay special attention to this training, but the degree of theoretical rigor is limited to what students can feel is necessary and can understand.

(2) Theorems that have been learned in junior high school should be dissected again using a heuristic method, and the method of inverse proof should be used as much as possible to clarify the path of thinking. The relationships between theorems should be used to form a system, showing the coherent thread of the entire geometry, so that students can grasp the key points and increase their ability to apply. However, the system should be based on theory to facilitate understanding and memory, and should not flow into rigid classification.

(3) Parts that have not been taught in detail in junior high school should be supplemented, and attention should be paid to the two parts of locus and construction problems. Therefore, in addition to reasoning and proof, these two parts can also develop students' ability to explore and invent.

(4) Geometric proofs and constructions should use algebraic methods as much as possible within the possible range to find the relationship between known components and unknown unsolved components.

(5) Solid geometry can only be taught in general terms, mainly to clarify the properties of equality and measurement methods, so that students can see through the circle on the plane and understand the structure of various solids, so as to be fully linked with the utensils used in drawing.

(4) Trigonometry: High school trigonometry should focus on trigonometric functions.

(1) Since acute-angle trigonometric functions and right-triangle solutions have already been learned in junior high school, high school can start with general-angle trigonometric functions for comparison and generalization. This not only seeks the universality of theory but is also necessary knowledge for those who study physics.

(2) The trigonometry taught in junior high school focuses on simplicity. High school should pay attention to the properties of trigonometric functions, trigonometric identities, equations, etc. (all should be compared with corresponding problems in algebra) for further study of higher mathematics.

(5) Analytical Geometry: High school analytical geometry should integrate algebra, geometry, and trigonometry to show where they are mutually useful. On the one hand, it serves as a general conclusion to the mathematics curriculum in secondary school, and on the other hand, it lays the foundation for advanced research.

(1) Analytical geometry should be mutually linked with algebra, geometry, and trigonometry to solve geometric problems and fully express the consistent nature of each part of mathematics.

(2) In order to obtain a corresponding relationship between graphics and quantities, it is necessary to use extended geometric elements. Therefore, analytical geometry cannot but differ from synthetic geometry (such as the problem of dividing angles). In all such places, it is best to make beginners pay attention to clarifying their views so that they are not confused.

(3) The scope of synthetic construction cannot be determined without analysis. If there is sufficient time, it is advisable to show construction impossibility (Lmpooodlecongtruction).

English

First, Objectives 164

(1) To enable students to practice using ordinary English that is practical.

(2) To enable students to get a glimpse of modern English literary works.

(3) To enable students to establish a good foundation for further study in specialized academic disciplines that require English as content.

(4) To enable students to open up a good path for further study in specialized academic disciplines that require English as a tool.

(5) To enable students to develop their language experience from the English aspect.

(6) To enable students to increase their interest in studying foreign cultures from the English aspect.

Second, Time Allocation 165

(1) Five hours per week.

(2) Time per week shall not be divided into certain hours exclusively for readers, certain hours exclusively for grammar, etc.

Third, Curriculum Outline 166

(1) First School Year

(1) Short selections, based on modern texts, whether full or abridged, must be mixed with narratives, descriptions, explanations, and discussions of various styles that have textual meaning, scientific colors, and other interests. Prose is the main form, and the language of poetry must be very close to the usage of prose (intensive reading, oral or written questions and answers, extracting key points, supplementing remaining meanings).

(2) Common application documents such as letters, constitutions, reports, etc. (reading, imitation).

(3) Common application formulas, such as social terms and business terms (ear-to-mouth practice, enactment).

(4) Systematized vocabulary, lexicon, and phraseology expanded from items (1), (2), and (3) (understanding, application).

(5) Systematized grammar expanded from items (1), (2), and (3), including the distinction and changes of parts of speech and sentence patterns (understanding, application). Note: Grammar is the old term for grammar.

(6) Selections similar to the teaching materials of items (1), (2), and (3), whether long or short, full or abridged, single texts or complete books, with no more than 8 or 9% new words. The amount used, including the teaching materials of the next item, must be at least three times that of item (1)'s intensive reading teaching materials (extensive reading outside of class, oral or written questions and answers about the content, drafting outlines, supplementing remaining meanings).

(7) Common periodicals such as daily newspapers and magazines (same as item (5)).

(8) Usage of special reference books such as thesauruses of synonyms and antonyms, dictionaries of place names and people, dictionaries of idioms, dictionaries of slang, and classified dictionaries (understanding, application).

(9) Various equivalent temporary teaching materials (use according to special learning motivations).

(10) Facts and meanings of foreign culture (especially those related to English-speaking peoples) that are convenient to point out in each item of teaching materials (understanding).

(2) Second School Year

(1) Same as item one in the first school year (add oral or written discussions, the rest are the same). (2) Same as item two in the first school year. (3) Same as item three in the first school year. (4) Same as item four in the first school year (add supplements, the rest are the same). (5) Same as item five in the first school year (add supplements, the rest are the same). (6) Same as item six in the first school year, with no more than 11 or 12% new words (add oral or written reports and discussions, the rest are the same). (7) Same as item seven in the first school year (same as item six). (8) Same as item nine in the first school year. (9) Same as item ten in the first school year.

(3) Third School Year

(1) Same as item one in the second school year (add imitation, the rest are the same). (2) Same as item two in the first school year. (3) Same as item three in the first school year. (4) Same as item four in the second school year. (5) Same as item five in the second school year. (6) Repair rules that are convenient to point out from the teaching materials of items (1), (2), and (3) (understanding, application). (7) Same as item six in the second school year, with no more than 14 or 15% new words. (8) Same as item seven in the second school year. (9) Same as item nine in the first school year. (10) Same as item ten in the first school year. Note: The new words in the above three school years total about 5,000 words (including about 8,000 words in junior high school). Approximately one-third of them do not necessarily have to be entirely based on the order in Thorndike's Teacher's Word Book.

Fourth, Summary of On-Site Methods 167

(1) Assignment Essentials

(1) Listening practice, (1) listening to understand meaning (2) listening to distinguish sounds. (2) Speaking practice, (1) speaking alone (2) oral questioning (3) oral imitation of sentences and paragraphs. (3) Eye practice, (1) silent reading. (4) Handwriting practice, (1) dictation of remembered words, sentences, and paragraphs (2) written imitation of sentences and paragraphs (3) free writing. (5) Listening and speaking practice, (1) oral imitation (2) oral answering (3) oral narration after listening (4) free conversation. (6) Listening and eye practice, (1) looking at phonetics or spelling while listening (2) listening to lectures while looking. (7) Listening and handwriting practice, (1) dictation while listening (2) note-taking while listening (3) written narration after listening. (8) Eye and speaking practice, (1) reading aloud (2) oral narration after reading. (9) Eye and handwriting practice, (1) copying words, sentences, and paragraphs (2) note-taking while looking (3) written narration after reading. (10) Eye, listening, and speaking practice, (1) oral imitation while looking at phonetics or spelling (2) asking and answering questions while looking.

(2) Key Teaching Points

(1) Within the scope of balanced development of listening, speaking, reading, and writing, special emphasis is placed on reading, making it suitable for the most common use of general students.

(2) All assignments should first be explained using clear methods so that students can accurately understand the real needs and have sufficient learning motivation.

(3) All exercises start from or end in complete sentences and paragraphs so that students can use sentences and paragraphs of language and writing.

(4) Pay attention to repeated practice to make it proficient.

(5) Fully review old lessons to make them permanently remembered.

(6) Encourage free application within the scope that students have already learned so that what they have learned can be related to life.

(7) Group practice and individual practice complement each other so that it can be popular and suitable for individuality.

(8) Use English more and Chinese less so that students can get more opportunities to practice and can learn more pure English.

(9) Often instruct on learning methods to increase learning efficiency.

(10) Always check whether students' work is correct and strive to prevent errors. Once discovered, correct them quickly and thoroughly so that errors that can be avoided can be avoided, and unavoidable errors do not become habits.

(11) Use special exercises and explanations to prevent or correct the most common mistakes of all students so as to economically solve the biggest difficulties of the whole.

(12) Always pay attention to students' grades so that you can adjust the progress of the program according to the predetermined plan.

(13) Often make students aware of their progress so as to stimulate interest and courage to learn.

(14) Except for those that cannot be avoided by using Chinese explanation, the meaning of new materials is generally expressed by other methods so that you can learn more pure English and reach the point of thinking in English as soon as possible.

(15) Gradually enable students to self-study new materials that have not been seen outside of class. Generally, self-study a small part of each lesson in the first year, a large part in the second year, and the entire lesson in the third year, so as to make full use of teaching time and gradually develop self-study ability.

(16) In addition to reviewing according to the original organization of each lesson in the old materials, it is also necessary to mix and reorganize the lessons for review so as to communicate, connect, change, and use them flexibly.

Spring Enrollment News of Suzhou Provincial High School 168

Suzhou Provincial High School is well-run and the largest in the province. The school's enrollment is divided into spring and autumn seasons. The number of classes depends on the number of graduates. At the end of this semester, there will be one class of high school and one class of junior high school graduates. Therefore, one new class of high school and one new class of junior high school will be recruited. However, since last year, the spring class of the high school department has only recruited chemical engineering students and does not accept general science students. Now, in order to meet the needs of society, in addition to recruiting one new class of high school and junior high school students in accordance with the regulations, 45 students will be recruited for remedial classes to facilitate the preparation of junior high school spring graduates for further education. Because spring graduates have difficulty in entering schools, many of them lose the opportunity to study. It is very strange not to remedy this situation. Therefore, the school has decided through a school affairs meeting on January 5 to add 45 remedial classes for relief. All recruitment regulations have been drafted. Those who are interested in applying can obtain them from the school. The examination period is February 2 and 3, and the registration period is from January 30 to February 1. It is said that those who request the prospectus are very enthusiastic.

Special Coverage

Respectfully Advise National University and Middle School Students to Practice Education to Save the Country (14) 169

— You Huaigao

In this era of scientific prosperity in the 20th century, no one should oppose the current government's construction policies. However, my suggestion is to ask the government not to forget that construction in education is more important than construction in material things. Because before most people in the country have received education, 99 percent of the construction is still bamboo fences and thatched huts, small boats and carts, simple and crude utensils, cloth clothes and cloth shoes. At most, only one in ten thousand people is engaged in scientific construction. As a result, it is just a drop in the ocean and does not help. Although it takes a lot of effort, the results are limited. If we can simultaneously carry out construction in education, we can increase the knowledge and change the thinking of hundreds of millions of people. Then, most of the people can assist the government in construction according to the standards of the 20th century. This construction is endless, universal, real, and great. The lost credibility can be compensated with education to the people better than using gold, silver, and wealth to relieve them thousands of times. Because gold and silver will be used up, the source of knowledge can not only be used up in a lifetime but also be passed on to future generations. Therefore, if the government really dares to issue this education service order to educate the people, it is enough to save the people from deep water and scorching fire. This is the benevolence of Confucianism, the compassion of Buddhism, and the love of Christianity. Therefore, we do not need to borrow gold, silver, and goods from foreign countries. We only need to take the seeds of wisdom from the brain bank of national universities and middle schools and spread them in the brain fields of millions of people. The harvest after ten years will be too numerous to count.

If our government can be built on faith and love, its foundation can make it impenetrable to water and indestructible to fire. It will be as stable as Mount Tai and as hard as iron and stone. Its life can be as long as the heaven and earth and the universe. This is what I earnestly hope from the current government.

In terms of the people, whether they are intellectuals, bourgeoisie, or farmers and workers, they should wholeheartedly support the current government, meet with sincerity, implement persuasion and advice, and abolish laughter, scolding, and conspiracy. In the period of national crisis, smart people should do their best, rich people should contribute their financial resources, and strong people should contribute their physical strength. This is the expression that the people should have for the country and the government.

Therefore, I hope that the government will use the word "faith" to treat the upper-class people and the word "love" to treat the second-class people. I also hope that the people will use the word "sincerity" to treat the government and the word "strength" to treat the country. This is a prerequisite for saving the country through education.

(18) Moths to Destruction and Bees and Butterflies to Save the Country 170

Everyone laughs at the moth's attraction to fire and calls it foolish. Everyone says that the fly is greedy for its pursuit of stench. But we are drunk and dreaming day and night, living in this world of sensual pleasures in Shanghai. Isn't this an act of moths rushing to the fire? There is also a group of people who, day and night, do things that deceive, plunder, conspire, and kill. Isn't this the fly's pursuit of stench? Although everyone has to die, they have to die at the right time. Why must they learn from the moth's rushing to the fire and die? Although everyone seeks a livelihood, they must seek it properly. Why must they learn from the fly's pursuit of stench and live?

We first compare a bee and a fly, and we can understand this principle. Look at a small bee. They cooperate and work together. They love the sun and enjoy working. They are diligent and thrifty. They know how to save. They can also plan ahead. Their honey comes from diligence and thrift. It is taken from the price of spreading pollen work. The physique of the fly seems to be similar to that of the bee in form, but in terms of spirit, there is a distinction between the worthy and the unworthy.

Let's compare a butterfly with a moth again, and this principle can be understood even more. Look at how butterflies love nature, flying and dancing among the green willows and bright flowers. They are both insects. The moth's unchanging attitude of sinking to death is completely different from the butterfly's clear, superior, and leisurely attitude. Therefore, butterflies can live out their years and complete their lives, while moths die out. This is the difference between wisdom and foolishness.

I believe that you are bees and butterflies who save the country, not flies and moths who destroy the country. Therefore, do not forget our great work of brewing honey. Heaven has given us a great source of power to feed our many ethnic groups. It wants us to use artificial brainpower, physical strength, group power, machine power, and time power to take this natural solar power, earth power, water power, electric power, and gas power in order to cultivate wealth and create happiness. Therefore, we are bees and butterflies who save the country. Then, this city is definitely not a place for us to carry out long-term work. Learning the behavior of flies and moths will at least turn into fly-moth-like bees and butterflies. This is the most painful and dangerous thing. Please pay extreme attention.

Our millions of square miles of land are the richest places for solar and earth power. For cultivated fields, improve the species. For uncultivated fields, develop them. For unopened mines, extract them. This is considered to be taking solar and earth power. The Yellow River Basin, the Yangtze River Basin, and the Pearl River Basin are the richest places for water and electric power. Use them to generate electricity, irrigate, transport, and raise things. This is considered to be taking water and electric power. Use chemical methods and the effectiveness of machines to carry out widespread manufacturing. This is considered to be taking gas power.

Eliminate this large block of illiteracy and illiteracy. Use a few wise men to teach the majority of the ignorant. This is considered to be using brain power. Save physical strength and give most farmers and workers appropriate entertainment and rest. This is considered to be using physical strength. Have a close organization and the virtue of working together. This is considered to be using group power. Widely use machines and cherish machines. This is considered to be using machine power. Lazy people must cherish their time and not be too relaxed. Diligent people must also save time and not overwork. And we must improve the system and look at the time. This is considered to be using time power.

Therefore, you should understand how great your responsibility to the country is and how heavy your affairs are. During this period of national crisis, we cannot allow countless useful bees and butterflies to stay in this city and imitate these greedy and foolish flies and moths to do some frivolous work and just be done with it. Therefore, if you want to save the country, you must resolutely leave Shanghai and go to the countryside in the interior to do the work of saving the country through education.

Report on School Hygiene Work Jointly Handled by the Two Bureaus of This City 173

The school hygiene work jointly handled by the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education and the Bureau of Health has been implemented for more than a month. The following is a record of the work report for December of the 21st year of the School Hygiene Division. The staff for December included one chief physician, one physician, one part-time physician, three school hygiene nurses, one dentist, and one dental nurse. The work for December included physical examinations of 3,006 elementary school students, identifying 4,394 defects, correcting 22 defects, vaccinating 258 people with cowpox, conducting morning inspections three times, providing ordinary treatment 147 times, and providing dental treatment to 31 people for 31 visits. Other work included (examining the physical fitness of personnel for the elementary school teacher certification of the Bureau of Education) 110 people. However, the actual number of dental treatments was more than this number because: 1. The number of return visits was not included. 2. The number of treatments for staff of the Bureau of Health and the Bureau of Education, as well as teachers from various schools, were not included in the records. Furthermore, the number of defects corrected was entirely from the dental department.

Student at Nanyang Commercial High School Retained for Cheating on Exam

Order from the Municipal Bureau of Education Regarding Appeal 174

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education issued an order yesterday to the privately-run Nanyang Commercial High School, stating: Upon investigation, the school held high school and junior high school graduation examinations on January 9th. This bureau sent personnel to supervise the examinations. According to the report, during the high school examination on domestic and foreign exchange, student Li Yi Wu, number 8, colluded with Huang Ruo Han, number 4, who was sitting next to him, to cheat. He should be immediately retained and not be allowed to take the graduation examination again, in order to deter others and maintain academic integrity. Furthermore, the teacher in charge of that subject arrived in the classroom twenty minutes late, which is highly inappropriate and should be reprimanded to emphasize the importance of examinations. This order is to be obeyed immediately.

On the school's two-year anniversary, a celebration ceremony was held at 10 a.m. at the Second School Building on Manufacturing Bureau Road. Attendees included Huang Tiren, representative of the Municipal Party Committee; Chairman Lin Kanghou; Tian Shouchang and Pan Yangyao, representatives of School Board Member Chu Minyi; guests Song Binqin; alumni Sun Mengyuan; and hundreds of others. After the rituals were performed, Chairman Lin Kanghou and Principal Wu Yuqian first reported on the hardships of the school's creation over the past two years and the future direction of its efforts. The speeches were quite detailed. Next, the Municipal Party Committee representative delivered a speech, followed by speeches from School Board Member Pan Yangyao and Chu Minyi's representative. The words were very sincere and moved the listeners. Finally, teacher representative Zhu Lin and student representative Jin Jiaoli gave speeches. A celebration amusement gathering was held at 1 p.m.

Junior High Department of Zhengfeng Middle School Relocates 179

Zhengfeng Middle School on Gordon Road has developed school affairs and the number of students has increased dramatically in recent years. The original school buildings are not sufficient. It is said that the school has decided to relocate the junior high department to the Western-style houses next to the Huangke Gymnasium on Seymour Road and Weihaiwei Road, which is run by the school's Principal Huang, starting next semester. Various facilities, such as books and instruments, have been purchased, in addition to some transferred from the school's high school department, to meet the needs of both departments. They are currently being arranged and renovated. As soon as the work is completed, they will begin operations at the new location.

Opening of Shanghai West Textile Night School 180

The China Textile Society, in order to train textile factory workers and young people aspiring to the textile industry and cultivate technical personnel for the textile industry, established the Shanghai West Textile Night School. Preparations began in December of last year, and students were enrolled on the 4th and 6th of this month, with 70-odd people admitted. The school is temporarily using Zhaoji Middle School in Caojiadu as its location. Classes started today. The opening ceremony was held in the auditorium of that middle school at 9 a.m. yesterday, with over a hundred people attending. Director Huang Yunqiu of the school presided, and Qian Guanyi avoided the ceremony. After the meeting opened as usual, the chairman gave an opening speech and reported on the preparatory process. Then, Society members Zhu Xianfang, Wang Yuxiu, Zhao Guoliang, and several students gave speeches, mostly focusing on striving to study, improving technology, developing the textile industry, and solving the clothing problem, one of the four major needs of the people's livelihood advocated by Sun Yat-sen, resisting foreign goods, and saving China. Finally, the chairman gave a speech, and the meeting adjourned after a group photo.

Diligence Bookstore Seeks "Elementary School Physical Education Textbook" 193

Diligence Bookstore, located opposite the Chinese National Sports Advancement Association on Laozhaoshenfu Road in Shanghai, recognizing that the nation is in crisis and that saving the situation requires a focus on physical education, is publishing a "Sports Series" with over thirty titles already available. Since its publication, it has been popular throughout the country. Because the teaching materials and methods for elementary school physical education in our country all need to be improved, we are seeking elementary school physical education textbooks, following the "Elementary School Physical Education Curriculum Standards" recently promulgated by the Ministry of Education, and offering substantial remuneration. The categories are as follows: (A) Grades 1-2 1. Story games, 2. Singing games, 3. Chase and escape games, imitation games, local games, and competitions; (B) Grades 3-4 4. Games (including chase and escape games, competitive games, imitation games, local games, and competitions), 5. Skillful movements; (C) Grades 5-6 6. Games (including competitive games, local games, and competitions), 7. Apparatus exercises, 8. Swimming training methods; (D) Grades 1-4 9. Imitation exercises; (E) Grades 3-6 10. Ball games and track and field training methods; (F) Grades 1-6 11. Dancing (including listening to music, movements, folk dances, and songs). All manuscripts that are well-connected before and after, as well as fragmented materials, are welcome. The remuneration is especially generous, and is not limited to the established practice of calculating by the word. The deadline for submissions is from January 10th to the end of February. Unsuitable submissions will be returned with sufficient postage.

Grain, Thin Rice Turns Soft, Little Activity Seen in Suzhou and Tongjing Rice Arrivals 216

Due to the small arrivals of Suzhou and Tonggang rice, sales were active, and the price was high by 1 "chi". Changbang rice was also short of goods, and medium-grade goods rose by about 1 "jiao". Yin Yuan and thick rice, Duyang Jian, etc., did not see much glory or disgrace. Spot inventory is weak. If the source does not surge, the market situation may have a chance to turn around.

(Zhabei) Yesterday, few boats arrived downriver. Wholesalers of white rice and shop sales were sparse. The market situation suddenly rose by 2-3 "jiao". There was continued source of early thin rice. Tianjin bulk sales were slightly digested, and retail sales were mediocre. The market surface was thinly determined. Early rice tightened by several "fen". Not much white yuan rice arrived, and sales were quite active, with prices rising nearly 1 "chi". Arrivals of Yin Yuan were low and sales were smooth, and the price carried a tight appearance.

Marked Flour Market Led by Spot Sales 217

Yesterday's flour market presented weakness in the morning. Western ginseng flour decreased by about 0.35 "jiao", and people's hearts for the near and distant terms were tired. Also, there were no major bullish absorption, and the declines from the previous close ranged from 7.5 "li" to 1.25 "fen". However, when the afternoon market opened, the hearts of people for near and distant terms suddenly became firm because the Northern customer gang continued to buy in batches, such as Tianjin and Yingkou, and Xinda opened 40,000 bags to be delivered at the Green Fort. The price was 1 tael 9 "qian" 4.5 "fen". Fuxin has been out of stock for a long time, and orders are scheduled for February. Fufeng still adds 8 "fen" according to the standard. Therefore, most people's hearts are tied to the smooth tightness of spot sales. Standard buying also became tighter. February, due to factory short covering, rebounded by 3 "fen" compared to the lowest price of the previous market. Because February will soon approach the price reduction of spot goods, the result was that this month was good by 7.5 "li", February was good by 1.75 "fen", March, April, and May were good by 7.5 "li", and June was unchanged.

Violet Orchid Convent Miscellany 259

— Recluse Cuckoo

Since the wooden clog-wearing cavalry trampled over the three northeastern provinces, more than a year has swiftly passed. Of the millions of soldiers in all of China, besides the 19th Route Army and the 5th Army, and the garrison at Yuguan, one cannot help but feel a sense of "not a single man among them." Fortunately, there are righteous soldiers who vow to resist Japan, enduring ice and snow as they fight the enemy. They have struggled for over a year, and countless patriotic heroes have sacrificed themselves for the country, their names unknown. We, who have survived them, want to comfort the souls of these nameless heroes, but we do not know where to begin! Yesterday, I discovered in an old manuscript a poem by the late poet Jiang Guanyun (Zhiyou), "Elegy for the Daring Ones, Past and Present." I hastily transcribed several pages, weeping towards the Northeast, bowing and burning them. If the heroic souls are aware, they will surely acknowledge these words as those of a discerning friend.

A noble man does not cling to life, and laughs at the butcher's knife.

The butcher's knife is sharp and flat.

In an instant, it is applied on the road,

Flesh and blood pickled in the mud and dust,

It is still better than being trapped in the source of the barbarian water,

As a bedridden, sourly moaning bitterly. (One)

Sharpen the knife again and again.

Hold it to kill pigs and sheep,

Sharpen the knife again and again,

Heroes mostly die because of this,

Sheep and pigs and heroes,

How can they not be divided in two,

Sheep and pigs are for food,

The human world is full of steaming and tasting,

Heroes are sacrificed,

The happiness of all beings is abundant. (Two)

A man embraces hot blood,

A hundred years waiting for a scattering,

Where is the scattering?

Green mountains and green history,

Green mountains give birth to brilliance,

The glorious events of the previous dynasty,

Green history gives birth to brilliance,

Flying high inspires people to rise,

Future fragrant people,

Butcherous drunkard of the time,

Butchering drunkard smiles,

Smiling, why bother with this? (Three)

Even if ants eat my flesh,

Ants also eat my fat,

Dogs also lick my blood,

Worms also pierce my bones,

I heard the words of the Buddhist family,

Using the body as alms,

If it benefits things,

Why is it not enough to describe it as a mess? (Four)

Straw mat as shroud,

Axe as containing jade,

Life values ​​heroism,

Not enough to fill the blessed shell,

You see heroic people,

Their spirit is still in their eyes,

How many are buried thickly,

Over the years, it turns into stone bones,

Stone bones sometimes run out,

Heroic names never fall. (Five)

Prisoners and executioners,

How respectful are they to me?

Hesitantly watching with affection,

As if surrounding their children and grandchildren,

What are you doing?

Not enough to say a word,

Right and wrong and merits and demerits,

Entrust to the discussion of all ages. (Six)

Cattle sometimes succumb to the yoke,

Mantis sometimes blocks the car,

The body of the ox is not small,

Muddy and boastful,

The body of the mantis is not small,

The spirit is like swallowing the remainder,

Valuing the people's spirit for the country,

The strong and the weak differ from this,

They strive for freedom to die,

Would they rather live as slaves? (Seven)

Dying of illness is the most unfortunate,

I used to say this,

Rotten scholars list the five blessings,

Examining the end is what the world gives,

Scholars value insight,

Future generations are like day rats,

Gentlemen nurture the great spirit,

The wise spirit relies on the great universe,

Strongly releasing the name of life and death,

Life and death, how will it come? (Eight)

Zai Yu's Daytime Nap - A New Interpretation of the Analects 260

— Cheng Luding

I dare not say how depraved Zai Yu was, I do not want to say how diligent he was, but I do not acknowledge Confucius' words as great truths. At the very least, Zai Yu had his own standards, didn't he? He was quite the modern college student.

Otherwise, why would he take a daytime nap? Although taking a daytime nap is not a sin, the daytime is a happy time, suitable for crawling like a dog in the girls' dormitory, or blowing things up in a classmate's room. Why sleep? What's so good about sleeping? He did not even breathe a little, so what was it for?

Was it to save the country, awaiting the dawn with weapons at the ready? Was it to resist the enemy, making night into day? I don't think so. Even if that was the case, at least it had nothing to do with studying.

Secondly, there's the dance hall, the amusement park, or some comfortable den, or perhaps a grand hotel.

In reality, rather than saying he was taking a daytime nap to save the country and resist the enemy, it would be more accurate to say he was taking a daytime nap while "saving the country without forgetting entertainment and resisting the enemy without forgetting entertainment." That would be more accurate and appropriate.

It can be seen that daytime napping has been "a constant since ancient times" in the history of college students, and of course, it is "even more rampant today." No wonder today's general college students are in love today and consorting with prostitutes tomorrow. It turns out that there is a basis for this talk.

The Rubber Hook in the Eyes - If You Are Hooked 261

— Ding

Rubber raw material rubber trees are produced in large quantities in Southeast Asia; however, the rubber hooks are produced in the eyes of every fashionable young woman. What strange news this is!

×× ×× ××

"Food and sex are the great desires of man." Even a sage like Confucius said this. No wonder the general youth who call themselves new people run on the wrong path of pursuing the opposite sex every day without fear of stumbling.

×× ×× ××

Traditional accounts tell us this: the place where women convey affection is in their water-cutting pupils. Indeed, this is undeniable. If women wear a pair of red glasses, even if the rest of them are intact and beautiful, all the beauty will be taken away by those glasses. Therefore, the first requirement of women is still in their flexible and moving eyes.

×× ××

Men are made of mud, so of course they will melt when they see women made of water. This is another kind of proof. If they often have opportunities to meet in a certain place, the rubber hook in her eyes will hook you completely in the invisible.

×× ×× ××

If you are hooked: your nerves will vibrate: there will be an image of a beauty in your mind; you will find work boring; you will feel that your family is outdated······and everything else. At the same time, you will be eager to: find more money for her to spend; steal some time to have fun with her. 丨丨Like this, from shallow to deep, from light to strong; you will finally enter the door of trouble and be unable to extricate yourself!

Humorist 262

— Ti Gong

(1) A friend traveled to Little Luzon during Christmas, a trip of more than ten days, costing more than a thousand gold. He returned a few days ago, looking haggard, as if he had recovered from a serious illness. Asked if he enjoyed the trip? He blushed and said: "Unfortunately, I had seasickness and lay down for days. There was no pleasure to speak of. Not only did I not see the soft hands of Luzon girls holding cigars, but I did not even catch a glimpse of the lights of Kowloon." This can be called a "humorous traveler."

(2) An amateur opera performer, invited to participate in a performance at an exhibition, brought a troupe of more than ten supporting actors. The scene was grand. Unexpectedly, the added drama was repeatedly delayed, leaving no room for intervention. Late at night, the performer quietly left. The person in charge did not know, nor did the supporting actors. I praised him as a "humorous amateur opera performer."

Rose-Colored Dreams

This is the trend of modern youth!

The Younger Brother of the Love Object

Ke is extremely tired of silence. People scolded him as a declining petty-bourgeois youth. But after a certain banquet, Ke suddenly changed his attitude and showed excessive affection for Jing. Fiction

Heartache · End · Red 264

— Lean Cuckoo

In this illusory film, some scenes are very clear, and some scenes seem to be somewhat blurred. However, no matter how old or small the matter is, not a single point is missed. This is what he experienced five years ago, and it can also be said to be a nightmare five years ago.

The first scene playing in his brain is a gloomy and terrible snowy night. That night the air was colder than iron; sharper than a knife, it forced the stars and moon to hide timidly. Goose palm-sized snowflakes, encouraged by the northwest wind, formed a large team, jumping disorderly in the air. The dead branches and leaves of the trees struggled hard in the cruel wind, issuing a series of mournful groans. In nature, there was a piece of darkness, occasionally borrowing the reflective light of the snow to show a tree and a house in the distance, all showing a hideous state, like many wild beasts squatting on the side of the road, baring their teeth and claws, ready to grab people and devour them.

At that time: he endured the cold; braved the snow; faced the wind like sharp arrows, panting; shaking; and with panic, he ran on a desolate and vast wilderness. He ran for more than ten miles in one breath, and still did not see a single person. Several times, he was almost knocked unconscious by the huge wind. The snowflakes all over his body, if turned into rice flour, would not only cure his current hunger, but would also be enough to store as food for a few days. His clothes and body were almost frozen into three whole pieces. But the colder his body was, the more anxious he felt, and the more he felt that this vast wilderness was exceptionally far away compared to when he had passed it in the past. When he slightly stopped to catch his breath, he only heard one or two dog barks in the distance, mixed in the howling wind, faintly floating to his ears. This kind of dog bark seemed unable to withstand this extreme cold, so it was extraordinarily sharp and urgent, equivalent to the last miserable cry of a patient dying. After hearing it, it almost immediately froze all the blood in his body.

It turned out that this time, because he was not tolerated by his dark family and his cruel stepmother, he gritted his teeth and would rather rush into the dark wilderness; cruel wind and snow, risking his life to go to his close friend Dongfangsheng.

When Ouyang Wu recalled the events of five years ago to this point, he suddenly felt a wisp of cold air冒出来直冒出来的，笼罩满了全身，彷佛又置身于当年的冰天雪阵中。

Children's Paradise

Why Do We Shiver When It's Cold? 265

— Bing Yu

Little brother, little sister, our bodies cannot be too cold, nor can they be too hot. If it is too cold, we will feel like shivering. Because in our brains, there are very sensitive nerves that pay attention to hot and cold. When the temperature of the body suddenly drops due to the influence of outside cold air, the nerves immediately send out an order to contract to the muscles in all directions. As soon as the muscles contract, they show a shivering appearance, so shivering is due to muscle contraction.

On cold days, if we exercise our whole body's muscles, we can generate heat. For example, if we stand still in a windy and snowy place, we will definitely get colder and colder. If we move our body and limbs up, down, left, and right for a few minutes, then the muscles in all directions will gradually tense, and the whole body will feel warm.

A Young Man's Invention 266

— Yun

Li Puman was a very poor young man. One day, he went out to travel and forgot to bring a rubber eraser, but he needed to write a travel diary. When he wrote his diary with a pencil on the way, he often made mistakes, but he didn't have a rubber eraser to erase them, and he felt very inconvenient. He thought quietly, if the pencil and rubber eraser were combined into one piece, it would naturally avoid this trouble. After returning home, he invented the method of attaching a rubber eraser to the end of a pencil. The "rubber-tipped pencils" that we use now are what this young man came up with.

There was also a Walter Hand, who went up the mountain wearing a cloak. Halfway there, the button of the cloak suddenly fell off. However, the wind was very strong on the road. As he walked, he thought, and came up with a method to replace the button. He took out a piece of iron wire, bent it into a curved shape, and made a safety pin. Later, he used this as motivation to invent the safety pin.

Ship Flags 267

— Chu

There are twenty-six kinds of flag signals commonly used on ships around the world, from A, B, C, all the way to Z. The language formed by their combination reaches 375,076 kinds. For example, the flag of C means "yes." The flag of D means "no." The flag of P means "goodbye." Combining the three flags X, O, R means "thank you." S, O, S means "help." This kind of language expression is the same for all ships in the world.

Finger Games 268

— Rui

Everyone, please watch me do a set of finger magic tricks for you:

(1) First, raise both hands in front of your chest, with the palms facing outwards and the thumbs pointing downwards.

(2) Move your left hand to the right side of your right hand and put your palms together.

(3) After crossing the fingers of both hands, squeeze them tightly and slowly rotate them downwards from the front.

(4) Squeeze both hands tightly and do not move, rotate them from below to the front of your chest. At this time, please recognize which finger is hidden in the opposite finger? Which hand is it?

Free Talk

Selling Children 270

— Fang San

"Who wants a child, selling a child!" A sad and high-pitched voice came from the alley into my room.

This is probably the saddest voice in the world! It is also the most indignant voice in the world!

Then, with one voice after another, high and low: "Who wants a child, selling a child!" Like a wounded beast wailing in the cold wind.

I opened the window and looked: a woman was sitting on the cement floor, wrapping a child in torn clothes. His mother seemed to be afraid that he would catch a cold, and also afraid that he would be snatched away, tightly holding him in her arms.

Next to the woman stood a man in his thirties, probably her husband, the child's father; the person who was shouting "Who wants a child, selling a child!" He lowered his head, his face full of sorrow and shame.

Five or six women were surrounding them, discussing the pros and cons. "This is not a good seed!" The Northern accent came from the mouth of a woman with permed hair wearing a cheongsam. Another woman, about forty years old, wearing Chinese clothing, but with smooth hair, combed into a cow-like bun. She said to the person selling the child:

"Can you write?" Hearing this, I thought she had a "good" heart and wanted to introduce him to a job. But then, she said: "You write a word, and I'll give you three or four dollars and sell me that child."

The man selling the child replied affirmatively:

"I can't. You can take him if you want, just give me a few dollars."

"It doesn't matter if you can't write, just draw a cross." She said again.

The man was hesitating, the woman holding the child was crying, and grief was gnawing at the hearts of a poor couple.

"It doesn't matter much whether you can write or not. Take a few dollars, and take the child away." After a long time, the man finally replied like this:

A woman pulled the woman who wanted to buy the child and whispered a few words in her ear. And showed a smug look: "It's not successful if you don't write."

The woman who wanted to buy the child said: "As long as you draw a cross, I can give you a few more dollars. You know, I still need to hire a nanny for him when I buy the child, and make clothes for him······" She showed a proud look.

Hearing these words, the woman holding the child cried even more sadly. Her head lowered to the child's head, her face lining the child's face. Intermittently said:

"Oh my god! Little precious, you······you; are you really going to be sold by me? I thought we could have food to eat when we came to Shanghai from the countryside, but who knew that after all the hardships of coming to Shanghai, we are still hungry···hungry···hungry. Your dad is going to sell you to eat! God, aren't we poor people even allowed to have children? Selling···selling···selling children·····" The sound behind was truncated in grief and anger.

His man raised his head, his face even paler and terrible; but what spewed out of his eyes was clearly the fire of anger. He said loudly:

"Are we still going to starve to death? Heaven, we are so poor that we are selling children, and we are not even allowed to have a child! But, we have to find a way to live! Poor people have to find a way to live!"

The women who were watching the excitement, seeing this crazy situation, all cast contemptuous eyes, and left like a swarm of bees, laughing and jumping. The woman who wanted to buy the child also put her hands in her pockets, gave a cold laugh, and leisurely went home.

The knife-like cold wind was still roaring in the air, blowing over the road, blowing over the wilderness, but it could not blow into the tall foreign houses. The parents who sold the child dragged their child, staggering and calling out on the road and in the wilderness. I seemed to hear him calling until dawn.

Let's Have the Facts 271

— Yang Xingzhi

Until now, our General Zhang Xueliang has finally gritted his teeth and said a "hard" word, "The Japanese atrocities can only be fought with flesh and blood, and justice can only be maintained with hot blood." (See the newspaper of January 9th) Although this is only a "word," it is "much better" than the attitude of always being "calm" and playing golf and listening to Peking Opera when there is nothing to do.

However, it has been a year and four months since the 9/18 incident broke out. We are used to hearing vows of "long-term resistance," and we are also used to hearing declarations of "preparedness," "planning," and "determination," and we are even more used to reading proclamations such as "the government will never fail the people·········" We have been deceived and fooled by such "vows" and "proclamations" for a year and four months. Now what we need are facts, standing up and working hard, and "really" taking blood and flesh to resist the actual actions of the Japanese atrocities. We no longer need smokescreens to deceive people, and we no longer need checks that are not cashed.

From retreating from Shenyang to Jinzhou, and then from Jinzhou to Shanhaiguan, now, the blood-red sun flag is flying on Shanhaiguan! Even if you can still retreat, but you retreat one step and he advances one step. The facts of the past year are as clear as iron. When you retreat, where exactly is your "last" "retreat"?

"Seeking self-defense and self-rescue through our own efforts" and "resisting the aggressive atrocities of Japanese imperialists" are "heavenly principles." As long as you are willing to "resist" and you are willing to "defend," the people will never let you fight alone. Ma Zhanshan, Cai Tingkai, Su Bingwen and other troops are examples before us.

The people will eventually rise up and settle accounts!

Dai Xiaohou Loses Weihai 272

During the reign of Emperor Guangxu, Anhui Hefei, due to Li Hongzhang's training of the Huai Army, following the Xiang Army of Zeng Wenzheng, conquered Hong Yang and pacified the various anti-Qing civilian armies in Henan and Anhui, so the famous generals of the Huai Army, such as Pan Dingzhen, Zhou Shengbo, and Liu Mingchuan, all became high officials. Most of these people were from the vicinity of Hefei. At that time, Hefei had a high reputation and commanded the Northern Ocean Army and Navy. At the time of the Boxer Rebellion, the Eight-Nation Alliance attacked Shandong and Zhili. The garrison commander of Weihaiwei was Dai Mingqian, with the courtesy name Xiaohou, from Shouzhou, and a student of Hefei. Dai commanded dozens of camps of the entire water and land army, and also led the various forts of Weihaiwei. At that time, the Beiyang Army had become the end of its strength, and Dai's personality was diligent in serving his superiors and cowardly in resisting insults. One day, Dai was gambling with his subordinates and lost a lot. A fort officer hurriedly came forward to report that there were several warships in the distance on the sea, and they were driving close to the fort. When viewed with a telescope, they seemed to be British warships. He asked for instructions on what to do. Dai was furious and scolded him, "You bastard; get out! Don't you know I've lost?" The fort officer had no choice but to return dejectedly. Before long, someone came in a panic again and urged him urgently, "Report to the Commander: The warships are about to reach the firing line, what exactly······" Dai scolded him angrily again, "Are you really blind? Just now I was losing, and you came to disturb me; now I'm just about to win, and you're bothering me again, are we enemies? Give me······" Suddenly, he heard, bang, bang, bang, and the enemy had already bombarded the fort. Dai pushed the cards away and fled without a fight. When the main general fled, the soldiers lost their fighting spirit, and the British warships easily occupied Weihaiwei. Afterwards, Dai reported that he had hanged himself, probably to deceive the Qing court to escape death. The complacency and martial arts of the Qing court resulted in losing the army and losing land in this way. How different is today from the past? Thinking about it, I am filled with emotion!

Mocking Eccentricity 273

— Wei XinSu

(1) Miers Watching Save a Life

The Scottish poet Miers (Robert Burns, 1759-1796) one day walked to the wharf in Greenock and happened to see a wealthy merchant fall into the river and be rescued.

After the merchant regained consciousness, he thanked the sailor who saved his life and solemnly gave him a shilling. The surrounding crowd unanimously condemned his stinginess, but Burns stopped them, saying:

"Let him be. This gentleman is naturally the best judge of the value of his own life."

(2) Button

The great German philosopher Kant (1724-1804) was an eccentric. When he lectured on the platform, his eyes were always fixed on a student whose coat was missing a button. This had become a habit. One day, the student's button was sewn back on, and the philosopher seemed to have lost his soul, and that day's lecture almost could not finish.

(3) Ireland's Tax-Free Air

One day, Lady Carteret, the wife of the Lord Lieutenant of Ireland, boasted to the Irish writer Swift (1667-1745) about the glory of Ireland. "The air of Ireland," she said, "is very beautiful and healthy."

"For God's sake, Madam," Swift knelt down to the noble lady and said, "don't say this in England, because if you say so, they will definitely impose a tax on the air again."

(4) The German Emperor's Design of a Warship

The German Emperor (Kaiser) liked to design his own palaces, castles, churches, and warships. In the 1910s, when he visited Italy, he became acquainted with Italian Navy Minister Admiral Bailing. Admiral Bailing was then regarded in Europe as one of the most talented shipbuilding experts. The German Emperor told Admiral Bailing that he could send him a drawing of a battleship, which he had planned with painstaking effort, a harvest of long-term research, tireless diligence, and contemplation.

A few weeks later, Bailing received the drawing sent by the German Emperor. After reading it, he returned it to the German Emperor along with the following letter:

"The warship designed by Your Majesty is truly the most capable, most terrifying, and most lovable battleship ever seen in the world. Its speed will definitely create an unprecedented record. Its armor can surpass all warships sailing on the water today. Its masts will become the tallest in the world, and its cannons will defeat any warship in the world. Moreover, the internal equipment is so perfectly arranged that all the crew, from the captain to the cabin boy, will enjoy being able to drive on this ship. This amazing warship has only one shortcoming: if it is put on the water, it will sink like a lump of lead."

Where Are the Farmers Going? 275

— Tian Fang

丨丨A Serious Rural Problem丨丨

Last winter, there was a great harvest in the country, with a yield of more than 120%. However, due to last year's floods and the invasion of foreign rice and wheat, as well as the manipulation of the market by merchants, rice prices plummeted. In Zhaozhu's hometown, 丨丨 the Jiaxing area of western Zhejiang, the recent rice price is only about five yuan per stone. According to the best harvest, calculated at three stones per mu, it can only be sold for fifteen or sixteen yuan. After deducting one-third for rent, the remainder is not enough to repay labor and fertilizer, let alone have surplus money to provide for wives and children to add clothing. Although rice prices are low, what other property do farmers 丨丨 especially Chinese farmers, have besides grain? Therefore, most farmers who urgently need money have to endure the pain of selling the grain they have worked for all year long. When they can no longer survive in the countryside, they come to the city to become industrial candidates. In this way, the rural economy is further declining, and the lower foundation of society is gradually showing signs of shaking. This collapse is becoming more and more obvious over the years.

The slogan "Establish the country on agriculture" has been sung in China for four or five thousand years, but in recent years, this old tune can no longer be sung. This is because agricultural countries import an average of 100 million yuan of foreign food. Isn't this a joke? Therefore, the old signboard of "Establishing the country on agriculture" has to be removed now. But the old signboard has already been removed, and the new signboard has not yet been hung up. If someone asks us what the basis of "establishing the country" is now, then we can only say that we are "establishing the country by relying on heaven." Because the old self-sufficient rural economy has been completely destroyed, and the new industry and commerce 丨丨 national capital is oppressed by foreign capital, making it difficult to rise. Now, in China's economic organization, the countryside has become the tail of urban industry and commerce, and urban industry and commerce have become the tail of foreign capitalism. The mode of production is not complete in our current tail. We are only gasping for breath in the cracks, and cannot find a way out. But this serious problem cannot be ignored. According to a survey by the Wuhan Central Land Committee in 1927, there are 336 million farmers in China, accounting for 84% of the total population. Most of these huge numbers of farmers have lost their livelihoods and cannot run to the city 丨丨 the city is also suffering the same fate. But survival is the first desire of mankind, and we cannot all starve to death. The two ways out for these farmers are to become "bandits" or "soldiers."

Becoming a bandit requires raising your own equipment, and the risk is great. The last way is mostly to become a soldier.

China is a country famous for its large number of soldiers, but in a society where "good men don't become soldiers," where do these more than two million strong men come from? The answer is that they are all surplus population forced out of the countryside.

Let's look at what happens after civil strife and war.

In theory, the responsibility of soldiers should be "defending the country" and "protecting the people." There should be no other definition, right? But in China, everything is an exception. Foreigners see Chinese armed comrades as tirelessly killing each other, which seems mysterious and too ridiculous. But this is the special characteristic of Chinese soldiers. Because they become soldiers due to extreme poverty, anyone who provides them with food and clothing is their benefactor. As for concepts such as "people" and "country," there is not even a shadow of them in the soldiers' minds. This is not surprising. Before becoming a soldier, life is extremely low. After becoming a soldier, life is extremely indulgent. This has created a special outlook on life, which is to believe in "omnipotent force." Wearing the skin of a tiger, who dares to say "no"?

How to Calculate Our Electricity Bill 278

— Xue Hai

Those who have been subtenants in Shanghai probably know the second landlord's wife's attention to the opening and closing of the tenant's lights, and the fuss about how much electricity is used, right? We often hear the second landlord's wife complaining that the tenant only pays one or two yuan for electricity, and a sixteen-candlepower lamp has to be lit until twelve o'clock every day, grumbling that the consumption of electricity is not enough for such a price. As for the tenants, they feel that the electricity bill they pay is more than enough; thus, a pointless dispute arises between the two parties. In fact, the second landlord definitely has no way to estimate how much electricity the tenant consumes each month; and the subtenant has no way to prove or explain how much electricity he consumes himself. Everyone speaks according to their own personal opinions, how can disputes be eliminated? Now I will write down some simple methods for calculating electricity bills, so that ordinary families can have a kind of preliminary calculation for the monthly electricity bill; and it can also avoid many disputes between landlords and tenants.

The size of the light we use now is calculated in "watts" or "candlepower." For example, if there is 40W on the light bulb, it is forty watts; or 32CP, it is thirty-two candlepower. Recently, light bulbs are mostly calculated in watts, and not in candlepower, because the watt unit is easier to calculate. For clarity, first copy a table below for comparison:

Wattage 7 5 14 5 18 25 25 40 60 100 150 250

Candlepower 5 10 16 18 8 31 34 88 88 70 1340 2270

We know that using one thousand watts of electricity per hour will move the electricity meter by one unit. Now we assume that a tenant uses a sixteen-candlepower lamp. We can find from the above table that a sixteen-candlepower lamp equals 18.25 watts. If the light is turned on at about six o'clock every day and turned off at twelve o'clock, averaging six hours, then the monthly electricity bill can be calculated according to the following formula:

30 × 6 × 18.25 / 1000 = 3285 / 1000 = 3.285 KWH

This 3.285 is the number of units on the electricity meter. Calculating each unit at twenty cents, the monthly bill is less than eighty cents! If we change to a forty-watt light bulb, we can also calculate according to the following formula:

30 × 6 × 40 / 1000 7200 / 1000 = 7.2 SWH

The calculation is seven units and some change, and the monthly electricity bill is only one yuan and forty-four cents.

With this calculation method, if more lights are lit, it can also be inferred accordingly. We should not be completely unsure about the electricity bill each month, right?

When they are bored in the office, or when they are dozing off at the counter, and think about the peaceful and leisurely scenes of the past few days, they can't help but hum "Where is it now?"

— A Group

Thank you for seeing Mei Lanfang's *Farewell My Concubine* and the Nanjing Grand Theater's *Savage Paradise*, and for also deigning to turn to this attached supplement; and for spending so much of your precious time to finish reading my "fart" of a text. I don't know what to say!

Dragging my tired body and mind, I prepared to rest in my small garret, but the news of the Japanese invaders attacking Peiping and Tianjin, once imprinted on my mind, never faded away.
