"Saving the nation" is everyone's business. Volunteer soldiers fighting the Japanese in bloody battles is saving the nation, the government's telegram for long-term resistance is also saving the nation, and even drinking tea, drinking wine, dancing... are all "saving the nation." I do my work, I eat my food, I don't become a traitor, I don't do anything that would let down the nation, society, or myself, so I can probably say I am passively "saving the nation."

Finally, you say that the residents of Shanghai have forgotten that the three million square li of Manchuria, seized by the invaders, are outside the pass. To donate a copper coin, they give it like alms to a beggar. That's why this recreational event for national salvation is being held. There's dancing, there's entertainment to watch, spending a few dollars doesn't matter. You, embracing the responsibility of "saving the nation," sacrifice your beauty and volunteer to participate. Forgive my rudeness for offending such a patriotic woman, no, madam. "Saving the nation" is just like this. Thank you for helping me break open this sealed jar. As the saying goes, hearing one sentence from you is better than reading ten years of books!

However, I must declare that the space in this publication is as precious as your dancing time. Whether you will see this letter when you turn to Mei Lanfang is still a question, so I solemnly declare that future letters will not be answered.

Life in a Dream 284

— Female Smoker

Busy with work all day, my body already feels extremely fatigued. The moment I lie down, I fall asleep with my head spinning. These days, I only wait for the arrival of sleep. Sleep is the supreme comforting realm for me. The pain I suffer during the day, whether given by society or self-inflicted; whether material or spiritual, can all be resolved in sleep. No, they can simply be transformed into vibrant red and white flowers.

Naturally, I have many sweet and grand dreams at night:

I myself don't quite understand how my originally weak body has become a heroic warrior, wearing a snow-white saber at my waist, holding a long bayonet rifle in my hand, stepping through the trenches of ice and snow, "Bang, bang, bang," shooting at the enemy. The enemies all fall down one by one in response, their fresh blood flowing into our trenches. I cup my hands and drink it wildly, singing patriotic songs in a loud voice.

Moreover, I also have a very beautiful lover with the same consciousness. She also carries a weapon and lies in the trench, shooting at the enemy. Her cheeks are flushed red, bathed in the blood of the enemy. Her legs are thick and strong, trained by running and killing the enemy. Sometimes I get impatient, and she comforts me not to be agitated. Sometimes I am timid, and she tells me to be calm. She says that after we recover the lost territory, we can have a fat child to remember it by.

Sure enough, the lost territory was recovered by us. Our nation was reborn. Manchuria is still our Manchuria. The suffering of the people is relieved, and my own pain has also disappeared. Everyone sings songs of victory.

"Woof, woof, woof!" The dog's bark echoes through the front of the window and the door. I wake up from my dream with a start, and touch my forehead. It's a handful of cold sweat. I am very angry at why I am still lying on this cold wooden bed, a useless corpse.

The dog keeps barking. There are hurried footsteps outside the window. The person next door is opening the door to relieve himself. "Ah, there's a thief, catch him quickly!" So the dog barks even more anxiously, but the footsteps fade away. I also become wary. But what does this have to do with me? Besides a few broken books on the bookshelf, what else is there to attract a thief? I think, how can thieves not be afraid of the cold? Fumbling around in the dark, they are just trying to prolong their lives. Their stomachs are hungry, what can they do?

The dog has stopped barking, but it makes me unable to sleep anymore. In the silence, I faintly hear the snoring of the fat boss of the silk shop next door. I think he may be having even grander dreams:

Trading what one has for what one doesn't have, who says Japanese goods can't be bought? Originally, doing business is to earn more money. There are car tycoons and oil tycoons ahead of us... setting an example for us. Who will come to investigate me? I don't care! Or I'll bribe some money to those poor kids, and that's it! If not, I'll simply change the labels and sell them. Anyway, all of our great citizens are greedy for bargains. You're good, I'm good, everyone gets rich together. If Manchuria is lost, what does it matter? The world is basically one family now. When I have hundreds of thousands of fortunes, donating a little is no problem. This is not the time!

The more I think, the more awake I become. The fat boss is as if shaking on the ceiling.

I get out of bed to smoke a cigarette, only to remember that I forgot to take in the leather shoes I put out to dry outside the door this morning. The dog's barking seems to be ringing in my ears again. I'm too lazy to open the door and look for them. Whether they're there or not is hard to say.

The cigarette doesn't induce sleep either, but makes my head even dizzier.

"Tick, tock, tick, tock," the pendulum of the clock, suddenly "Dong, dong" rings five times. I open my eyes and look out the window. The sky is already the color of fish belly. So I put on my clothes, jump out of bed, and continue to busy myself with my work.

Shop Employee Communications

To Transform the Environment, One Must First Have Organization 285

— The Editor

Among the many letters received from readers, the majority express the need for collective unity. Therefore, many letters regarding the organization of groups have already been published in this column. However, organizing a group is not an easy task, and especially organizing a perfect group.

Currently, as far as we know, there are already three groups that have the beginnings of a group and are already starting; this is only based on the perspective of shop employees, workers, apprentices, and those related to them. They all have great perseverance and an indomitable spirit; although it is not yet possible to say whether they will succeed in the future, we must at least know that the success of an organization is based on the spirit of the organizers and the core members.

For an organization with a pure purpose, although we cannot be in a leading position to work hard to preside over it, the responsibility of assisting from the side is our inescapable duty. Therefore, we hold a sincere hope that they will succeed soon, make contributions to society, and benefit the people. At the same time, we also express our admiration for the shop employees, workers, and apprentices who have far-sightedness, feel an urgent need, and therefore automatically rise up to organize, and are able to overcome all difficulties and gradually move towards the path of success!

Before introducing these three groups to the readers, we would like to offer a little advice to express our encouragement and mutual encouragement; "Failure is the mother of success" is a famous saying that you all know. If you encounter obstacles or suffer blows in the future! You must not be discouraged. At that time, you must remember this famous saying, continue to work hard and strive; you must know that the greater the blows you receive, the more solid the foundation will be in the future. The following is an overview of the three groups.

(1) Youth Work-Study Society In their declaration, they say; "... After the ceasefire agreement was concluded, all industries were depressed, and the people were struggling to make a living; we know even more deeply that unless we fundamentally and practically handle labor education to increase the wisdom of the people and promote the spirit of the people, our Chinese nation will not be able to plan for internal stability and resist foreign aggression and survive in the world. ... Everything that is most practical and beneficial to society is generally the most difficult to succeed; if we know the difficulties and plan for them in advance, then it will be easy to proceed. ... Moreover, now that we know the difficulties and move forward, we will never retreat when we see difficulties in the future. ..." From this, we can see that they have "the heart to succeed" and are "thinking before acting." They implement "labor education" with precise plans. Their purpose is "to promote the combination of manual and mental work"! Gradually achieving "no manual laborers who do not study, and no idlers who do not work." Moreover, they already have a considerable financial base, with Penglai Market as the area of implementation, and then gradually expand it. The founders, Kuang Zhongmou, Zhou Zhaoji, and others, are very enthusiastic. The location is at the Alumni Association of the Chinese Vocational School in Xiaoximen.

(2) Amateur Academic Research Society This organization is slightly different from the first organization. The first organization is the cooperation between labor and management to seek reform of the social system, so the plan is relatively grand. This organization is entirely because shop employees and others feel panicked about their own knowledge and use their spare time to make active remedies, so its scope is limited to "academic research" and mutual assistance in spirit. The process is also simpler. They wrote in their letter; "... Although it has not yet been formally established, there are already a considerable number of people, and the preparatory meeting has been held three or four times, and the charter has also been drafted. We are now recruiting members extensively, as long as they are formal shop employees, workers, and apprentices, they can join. ..." They also said; "... The liberation of shop employees themselves must have sufficient knowledge, and we can only do it by pooling our efforts ... We changed the name from "Weekly Academic Discussion Society" to "Amateur Academic Research Society" because it was too narrow. ..." The initiators are Zhang Siwei and others, and the address for correspondence is Zhang Siwei c/o Hezhong Enterprise Company, P.O. Box 2049, this port.

(3) Workers' Autonomy Advancement Society This organization and the second organization are on the same position and have the same meaning, but the scope is more extensive. Their letter said; "... Since I am not a person of great wisdom, I might as well use my stupid brain to do some stupid work. At the same time, I also feel that my strength is small, but there must be many such small forces in society ... I am determined to start from today, do it down-to-earth, gather these many small forces, and organize them into a group. The name of this group is "Workers' Autonomy Advancement Society" ..." We greatly admire this firm spirit. They have also predetermined plans for industrial manufacturing, academic research, cooperative undertakings, proper entertainment, travel, etc. The founder is Liu Xinmin, and the location is 164 Xinkaihe, Min'guo Road.

We know that to transform the bad system of society, we must first have organization, and we need a strong organization, so that we can achieve the goal of a good environment. The above three organizations are the beginning of the transformation of the environment. We hope that everyone will continue to work hard and complete this major mission as soon as possible.

Novel

The Sympathizer (14 Continued) 286

— Zhang Henshui

Wang the Second, the rent rice account from last year hasn't been settled until this time of year, that should be good enough for you, right? You still owe four dan and five dou of rice. No one needs to mention the five dou, I'll let that go. As for the four dan, do you want to pay in cash? Or do you want to give me rice?" Wang the Second loaded a dry tobacco pipe, leaned against the windbreak wall by the steps, and said slowly in a very dejected manner, "I beg the landlord elder to have mercy. With last year's harvest, that area couldn't possibly yield a full rent." The landlord said, "According to you, should I just let go of these four dan of rice?" As he spoke, he flipped through the account book again, as if examining it, and shook his head, "No way! None of my tenants have ever been let off this much." So these people who had eaten the landlord's food had an obligation to mediate and all came to persuade. After everyone discussed, Meng Guobao interjected, "My father is also a landlord, I won't be biased towards either side, I'll speak fairly. When the new rice came on the market last year in August and September, it only sold for three or four dollars a dan. When the landlord came to collect the rice, the tenants had rice. After April this year, rice sold for five or six dollars a dan, and the tenants' rice at home had already been sold. At this time, if you want to collect rice, the tenants naturally don't have it. If you want to convert it to cash, compared to last fall, the tenant has to lose more than two dollars per dan of rice. How can farmers bear that?" The landlord's face turned red and he said, "According to Mr. Meng, it sounds like the landlord deliberately waited until this day to settle the accounts. But I don't know that I urged him to settle up last fall, but he never settled it. What can I do? If it's not settled, the new rice will come out again." Wang the Second said, "It's not that I didn't settle it, but I already lost money on the rent rice I gave last year. Where am I going to get it for the landlord?" Meng Guobao said, "Old Second, you're also at fault. Last fall, after you gave all the rice, you should have stated that you couldn't give any more rice. But it's not enough to just state it to the landlord, because even if you say you stated it to the landlord, the landlord might say you didn't state it, so it's still not clear. You should report this to the district office. The gentlemen in the district office now are all young students, they will definitely speak fairly." As he said this, every sentence was telling Wang the Second, but his voice was very loud, clearly telling the landlord.

Film Special

January 11, Year 22 of the Republic of China. Wednesday (No Additional Charge)

New Movie Preview

The Barrymore Family's Collaborative Masterpiece 287

— Brilliant

The Barrymores are known to everyone as the only family in the American art world worthy of admiration. In Hollywood, there is no other family more glorious or revered than them. Although I only know three big stars from their family on the screen now—Lionel, John, and Ethel—there must be countless members of their family serving in the film industry, and many of their ancestors were famous figures on the stage. Even now, there are still many Barrymores in Broadway. Therefore, the art world of the United States regards them as "The Most Royal Family of America."

Despite this, the Barrymore's family reputation is also very mysterious. They have very little contact with the outside world. News reporters are even less welcome. Therefore, what people know is only that they love art. Their homes have extremely rich libraries and extremely luxurious storage rooms. They have bought countless sculptures, antiques, and famous paintings, but no outsiders have ever been inside to visit. Recently, their attitude has changed somewhat, and they often hold grand banquets, but the only places guests can go are the magnificent living rooms, dining rooms, and gardens in their homes.

In films, they have always been independent of each other, striving for their own great careers. Although they live together, their lives are also very clearly separated.

Last year (1932), when there were major changes in the film industry, they had to cooperate on the screen. The first time was *Arsène Lupin* (already shown in Shanghai), and the second time was *Grand Hotel* (scheduled to be released in Shanghai in early March). The release of these two films has been welcomed around the world and has further increased their honor. In fact, this was only a collaboration between Lionel and John.

They recognized the path of modern art, and only cooperation can lead to greater success, so this recent collaboration has added Ethel. The name of the new film is *Rasputin*. It tells a Russian story, which was chosen by the three Barrymores themselves. Lionel plays an elderly and mysterious monk, John plays a great soldier of the empire, and another protagonist is a noblewoman, which is perfect for Ethel. With these three big stars playing these three equally important roles, the results will definitely be amazing. Moreover, the scenery and costumes are extremely realistic. It is said that MGM sacrificed a great deal for this film. People in the company believe that this is the only blockbuster after *Grand Hotel*. However, Ethel's eyes have not been very good recently, and she is unwilling to be too stimulated by the carbon arc lamps, so she only works for a very short time each day. This means that *Rasputin* will have to be completed at a later date.

Film Gossip

Recent Fashion Trends in Hollywood 288

— Luo Fen

Probably in the summer of last year, Joan Crawford and Lili Damita started wearing bangs on their foreheads, which was considered fashionable for a while. Women in Hollywood followed suit, working hard with mirrors and scissors every day. Now Constance Bennett has invented a new type of bangs, which is a bunch of short hair, permed into a crescent shape, hanging on the left side of the eyebrow. When she first wore this style while filming RKO's new film "Rockabye," she was praised by the public, so many people followed suit, treating it as the most fashionable decoration.

Currently, the most popular fashion among women in Hollywood is a pointed felt hat. The reason why this felt hat is popular is because Ann Sothern received extremely high praise for wearing it in the film "Let's Fall in Love," so every Saturday afternoon, no fashionable woman in Hollywood is without this felt hat. This hat is called Mickey Mouse Hat in the United States and Breton Hat in the United Kingdom. It comes in various colors. Ann Sothern wears a brown one. Country girls used to wear this kind of hat, but unexpectedly, it has now become the darling in the eyes of fashionable people.

Wu Suxin's Way of Supporting Her Husband 289

— Ji Zhong

Zhang Huimin and Wu Suxin have a deep and affectionate relationship. Since Huimin Chinese Drama Company declared bankruptcy, Suxin has been worried about it. Later, during the January 28th Shanghai Incident, they risked filming "The Glorious History of the 19th Route Army." It was shown in various places inside and outside the port, and was very well received by people from all walks of life. Now Huimin and Suxin have decided to temporarily suspend the Huimin Chinese Drama Company and re-establish a new company, named Huimin. Recently, they have been actively proceeding and starting to shoot a film. The plot of the new film is still based on martial arts and love as the main themes, named "A Strange Encounter on a Desert Island," and has been completed to about 30 or 40 percent so far. Suxin has put in extraordinary efforts. Commentators say that Wu Suxin has a way of supporting her husband, which is indeed true.

The evening coat worn by Gwili Andre in the film "A Man's Mate" has elastic bands inside the clothes that can be stretched. The sleeves, which are invisible from the outside, are tight, and the cuffs are trimmed with a piece of leather. Everyone marvels at Gwili's cleverness. This kind of coat is called the champion of clothes, and it goes without saying that many people follow suit.

RKO star Mary Mason has recently been wearing a clever ring that can hold a photo inside. This has shocked the entire city of Hollywood again. If a fashionable man doesn't have a woman putting his photo in her ring, this person can be thrown into the Pacific Ocean.

Recently in Hollywood, a kind of woolen clothes worn for playing ball is popular, and the style worn by Fay Wray is the best. In the past six months, Fay Wray has prepared many of these woolen clothes, and she gives one as a gift whenever her friends have a birthday. But if you ask her for one, she will never give it. So her friends are looking forward to their birthdays coming soon.

Joel McCrea's clothes are now considered the most fashionable among men in Hollywood. He wears a British-style suit with leather buttons. Men in Hollywood are all wearing clothes made to imitate his style.

Tianyi's Military Reorganization 290

— Xi

The two brothers Shao Zuiweng and Shao Cunren, the owners of Tianyi Company, in order to promote amateur sports for their employees and actors, have specially equipped a sports field very completely, with swings, see-saws, seesaws, wave boats, horizontal bars, etc. In addition, they have also organized basketball and football teams. The basketball team once had a friendly match with the basketball team of the China Wireless Radio School, and the result was undecided. On the afternoon of the 8th of this month, they will have a second match at the company's stadium. Shao Lao specially allocated a sum of money to prepare brand-new uniforms for the team members and purchased an American top-quality basketball. In addition to the original members Tang Xiaodan, Ma Loufen, Hua Ling, Zhang Zhenduo, Bao Zhichao, Li Xiongxiang, Fu Jiqiu, Wu Weiyun, Tian Fang, etc., Hu Yipei, Chen Shaoxian, Chen Yaorong, Chen Guanqian, etc. have recently joined. Recently, the team has been practicing very diligently during their spare time from work.

This is the sweet star Ann Sothern and her daughter Patricia. We met Ann Sothern in the film "Let's Fall in Love" the other day, but Patricia is not unfamiliar either. Look at her face, isn't she a little Ann Sothern?

Star Anecdotes

Jean Harlow's Anecdotes 291

— Mei Cun

Jean Harlow, the protagonist of "Three Wise Girls," is from Kansas City, Missouri, USA. She is now twenty-two years old.

Her father was a carpenter. When she was thirteen years old, her father died. For the sake of her future, her mother and she moved to Hollywood and rented an apartment there. At that time, there was an actor named Wyndham Standing who had just arrived in Hollywood from England to work in films. He also lived in this apartment, so they became acquainted with each other through frequent meetings. This was her first time approaching film industry figures.

Once, she went to Fox Company to find a friend. Because of her moving beauty, the friend took her to see the director. When the director saw her, he asked her to be an extra. Later, she was recruited by Hal Roach Company and signed a five-year contract.

A year later, Howard Hughes was about to start filming "Hell's Angels." The protagonist at the time was a beautiful Norwegian woman named Greta Nissen. After completing part of her work, she had to go to New York due to a contract with a certain stage, so a protagonist was missing. Hughes could not find a replacement among hundreds of actresses. At that time, James Hall and Ben Lyon (who played a young soldier in the film) happened to meet Jean Harlow and happily introduced her to Hughes. Hughes was very fond of her, and Jean's name became a sensation.

In July of this year, she married Paul Bern, and on September 6, Paul committed suicide. She suffered great grief. Recently, she has been filming "Red Dust."

Han Yunzhen After Marriage 292

— Qingxia

Han Yunzhen, everyone knows she is a veteran movie star; about six or seven years ago, her name was perhaps no less than that of Hu Die today. She acted in many plays, and because she was good at playing romantic roles, someone gave her the nickname "Sau Sister."

Since she left the film industry and got married, she developed an addiction, and her spirit became very weak, and her body was also very frail. The "beauty and health" of the past has been thrown to the winds. With a thin and pale face, no one would believe that she was the once-renowned Han Yunzhen in the film industry.

Her husband often advised her to quit; she also hated the addiction; and cursed her own absurdity. Therefore, she made up her mind to quit the addiction.

Now, she has quit her addiction, and her body seems to be much stronger; although she is already middle-aged, her former demeanor has been restored. She is almost ecstatic. According to reports, she may soon return to the screen as Feng Fu. Let us wait and see what happens next!

The Face of a Born Klutz 293

— Xin

Aubrey Smith was born with uneven eyebrows. When he was working on the film "Of Human Bondage," he only had to stick on a fake mustache and didn't need much makeup, but he already had the face of a klutz. When the film was completed, Lubitsch joked to him, "Go home and wash the paint off your face, and take off those ugly mustache and eyebrows. Otherwise, no woman will love you."

Kissing Wax People is Not a Crime 294

— Ai

Playing Bridge is very fashionable in Hollywood. Once, three female stars asked Chico Marx (one of the four Marx Brothers) to join them for a game of Bridge, but stated that there would be no money involved. Chico said that playing Bridge for small stakes is like kissing a wax woman, it's meaningless. One of the female stars immediately said, "But forcibly kissing a wax person is at least not a crime, right?"

The Skills of the "Match King" (5) 295

— Translated by Ximeng

Paul Krüger still used his beauty trap. A Miss Sanya was seduced by Paul and gave her heart to him. But Paul introduced her to Mr. Rodinski, a Polish banker. Rodinski was the Polish government's chief financial officer. So Paul arranged the spider's web and hid aside to wait for the opportunity. Rodinski rented a small house for Sanya in Warsaw, the capital of Poland, and decorated it like a fairy palace. It was exclusively for his personal entertainment in his spare time, and Sanya was considered his bedroom.

One day Paul went to Warsaw to visit Sanya. She said with a smile, "Paul, you are a liar, you are going to tell me many sweet words again."

"My dear," Paul's voice was very low, he embraced Sanya in his arms, his heart was pounding so hard that it could almost be heard, and his face showed many emotions of parting, more real than real. "If words could describe the pain of not seeing you... you will never know how many times I wanted to put aside all my business, regardless of Stockholm, London, New York, Paris, all the banks, railways, factories, just to come to you here." He kissed her hand, he knelt beside her, hand in hand, eye to eye. "What I am doing is for our future, so that we can never be separated and enjoy the happiness of peace." He stood up and kissed Sanya passionately.
